delicate

“you can only run so far from a past this dark.”

01:00 | best friend

"Fuck, fuck, fuck!" She was whispering to herself in exasperation, running down the halls of YG entertainment. Her footsteps were quick and loud as her converse clicked against the wooden floors where she was located on the fifth, her green eyes darting in every which direction.

It wasn't unusual for her to be late to work, at least not recently. The truth she was a little ashamed to admit was the fact she had gotten a bit more — distracted — from her career than she'd liked. Although she wouldn't say the fact she got highly intoxicated and ended up doing some uncalled for things with another idol was her fault, it was also definitely her fault.

Such an unplanned event that happened all those nights ago in the cold month of October had ended up becoming a regular thing — almost too much of a regular thing. It was the solemn reason she kept ending up late to her recording sessions because she would end up sleeping in due to the 'rough' night she'd had, then she'd end up late to her recording session all over again. 

No matter how many times she asked him to wake her when he woke up to come to the studios, he never did. Of course, whenever she confronted him about it he always said the same thing, "I try, but you're seriously a heavy sleeper."

Stressed from the fact she was in deep shit, the brunette runs a hand through her disaster of hair. The staff gave her worried looks as she passed them, definitely noticing the usual angel of YG was absolutely out of whack.

They weren't exactly wrong for thinking so, either. All the stress of her job was building up on her, and what she was doing with him was one of the only ways she knew to try to get rid of it.

But the fact that doing that kept ending up with her being late absolutely was not helping her case.

The small girl was exhausted by the time she finally reached the studio, due to the fact she had ran like a mad man the entire way. Looking at her reflection in one of the windows, she tried to at least barely fix the mop atop her head. After a second, however, she'd deemed it was hopeless.

Knowing there was no way she would end up making herself presentable, she'd shrugged to herself as she grabbed the handle. It was cold against her fingertips, and she forced a smile onto her face as she prepared to face her manager on the other side.

Who she hadn't expected to meet — was them of all people.

The seven boys eyes widened at the sight of her. Her green eyes bulged as she saw how their eyes went from her hair, to her dead expression, all the way to how she probably looked like a zombie. It was when Bobby turned his head to try to hide his snicker that the others joined in, and she felt herself having a hard time resisting the urge to kill them all on sight — including him.

"Seems like you and Jinhwan almost had too much fun," Junhoe had hummed as he stifled the laugh he so badly wanted to let out at the poor girls state

The maknae had sighed as he looked to the boy, "no shit, you could hear it through out the entire apartment," he winced as he spoke the words, "it was fucking traumatizing."

Clenching her fists at her sides, she didn't even get a chance to yell at the boys who were making her life more of a pain than it already was. It was clear her staff that were going to help her record had left the studio as it must've been time for iKON to use it. The guys were either lazy, or just taking a break from the difficulty that recording was.

Either way, she didn't sign up to deal with their bullshit. Not when she had only been awake for a maximum of two hours.

As they began laughing and making fun of the noises they heard from her, she found her cheeks growing bright red and her veins flowing with fire. Just as she opened her mouth to scream at them, she heard a voice that was strong enough to cut through all the others. It was one that sounded like pure bliss, that seemed to sink deep into her eardrums and soak them with her favorite scent of cherry blossoms. Such a sound was enough for her to close her mouth, her eyes jolting as he grabbed her full attention just like that.

"Soomi, just ignore them," Jinhwan sent her that grin that she loved so desperately, opening his arms towards her as he cooed, "come here."

Just like that, was the reason she could never be mad at him even if she wanted to be. Stepping forward a few steps, she fell into the arms of the place she'd grown so accustomed to since October. It was a place she felt safe in, and one she didn't want to leave no matter how dangerous it really was.

They knew it was bad. You weren't supposed to be with other idols or other people romantically period. It was dire to your career, and if anyone like the fans and especially the CEO found out — it's over.

It was why the two were usually so secretive, but then, they had had too hard of a year, too hard of a day. They didn't have the energy to worry about anything else than the warmth of each other.

Jinhwan's arms felt secure around her waist as she buried her face in the crook of his neck. Her lips left a short, lingering kiss there as if to tell him how she was thankful for him. It was a pleasant moment that was once again, broke by the idiots laughing in the background.

In the fits of their giggles, Donghyuk had worriedly questioned, "aren't you both worried about getting caught?"

He wasn't trying to ruin their moment at all. Donghyuk (and beloved Yunhyeong) were the ones Soomi could actually really get along with out of the members of iKon that didn't consist of Nani. She could tell he was just thinking of the reality, and the fact that them being so clearly affectionate with each other — especially in the studios — was dangerous.

It was true, at any moment a staff even as simple as a janitor could walk in. From there, both of their cherished careers would practically be dead for. If anyone found out, it would be the end of everything they knew so well.

However, with all the weight on her shoulders recently, Soomi wasn't quite sure if she even cared in the first place.

The laughter and making fun of their hyung had eventually died down, as everyone was beginning to think of the truth that there was to Donghyuk's question.

Soomi didn't have the energy to speak from where she was hidden in the safety of his hoodie. Jinhwan had sighed as he bit his lip nervously, unsure of what to say to the matter. Of course, he knew the obvious well. Everyone knew the harsh rules of the industry.

"It's okay," he was careful with his words as they slowly left his lips, "we aren't technically together."

Bobby had snorted humorously from where he was leaning back in the leather couch that was outside of the recording room, "bullshit."

Annoyed with the attitude, Soomi had sat up from where she was getting rather comfy. The frustration radiated off of her, making everyone aware especially due to the expression on her face as she turned to face the six boys. Their eyes turned fearful as they watched her remove one of her converse. With a swift motion, she winged it straight at Bobby's head.

The boy had been the only one who hadn't been paying attention, which was why it had hit the top of his head harshly. Such a sudden impact caused a yelp to leave his lips as he jumped in the leather seat, looking down to where the shoe had fallen.

"Fuck, alright, I'm sorry!" He was crying in defense, because as soon as he looked up, the same girl was standing right before him with flaming eyes, "I get it, you're not really together."

Soomi only sent him a salty, close lipped smile as she picked up her shoe. Walking over to fall onto the seat beside Jinhwan instead of on his lap, she bent over to put it back on.

"Jinhwan is just — my best friend," She hummed as if it was no big deal as she was sitting back up.

The others eyes were confused as they stared at her, before looking to their hyung. Jinhwan wasn't paying attention to anyone, his brown eyes were heavily fixated on his feet. Not a word left his lips, and they worried that he might not have the same thoughts about their relationship that Soomi did.

Until finally, he cleared his throat, "yeah, we're just best friends."

It was one of the dumbest things any of them had ever heard. Jinhwan practically only spoke about the poor girl whenever they had free time, that was, if she was actually there with them. Soomi lived in the same apartment complex as the boys of iKon, but she spent most of her time in their apartment instead of her own.

They knew how their hyung really felt for the female idol, even though he hadn't said it himself. There was no way they couldn't know with how obvious he made it.

But the words she spoke made it clear she must not feel the same. It was sad to see they were just 'using' each other for stress relief, or at least that's what Soomi thought.

They felt bad for Jinhwan, as they watched him shift uncomfortably in his seat.

A long, awkward silence filled the recording waiting room. It was one that made everyone want to sink into the ground to never be seen again, until someone finally broke it.

"So, I'm guessing you were late for your recording session again?"

The still tired girls green eyes had met Hanbin's, and she let out a deep sigh at his question.

"You guessed it."






02:00 | freedom

"Soomi-ah," the CEO of one of the largest entertainment companies in the entirety of South Korea's eyes were stern but sincere as he peered into the green irises of her own, "you can't keep messing up your schedule like this and ignoring the staffs calls. If there is something going on, tell them, and we can arrange for you to take some time off, but you cannot keep horsing around. It's letting down not only yourself, but your fans." His words were more heartfelt than she expected, due to the known fact that CEO YG wasn't always the nicest person around. Especially with the way she'd been recently regarding her job, she was surprised that he was being so genuine. 

Then again, it didn't take her long to understand why. For the last three years, all she'd been doing was working non-stop. After all, being an idol had been her dream ever since she'd watch them on TV growing up. The moment she saw Big Bang on television, she knew exactly where she saw herself. And to the halls of YG Entertainment she'd went, after years and years of practicing to make the perfect audition, and even more endless hours of training to then make the perfect idol.

It'd been a long, sweaty road she'd embarked on. Sure, she painted this image of where she wished for herself to be, but never did she think of everything she would have to do to get there.

After practically starving herself to lose weight to be fit enough so she could fit the correct standards, and making sure she was in good enough shape to be able to with-hold her stable vocals while still doing the correct dance, she'd made it. It'd taken countless music banks, promotion shows, and TV appearances, but she was here. She was where she always wanted to be.

As one of the largest female solo artists in all of Korea, everyone envisioned her as some sort of goddess. With the fame brought stress, and she had never once stopped to think about how it would affect her and her mental health.

Soomi had always thought that once you made it to the top, you have it easy from then on. It'd been the largest wake up call she could've dreamed of once she actually got there, only to find out you had to work even harder than you did to get there to stay there. The demand for her music and appearances only rose as her popularity did, so much that she felt as if the entirety of the country was on her shoulders. 

It was why she looked to other things to try to weigh out how empty she was feeling. Her schedule was only getting tighter and tighter with the fame she was gaining, to the point where she was losing her sanity. It was why she started missing so many schedules, delaying her rehearsals, ignoring the staffs calls - but most importantly - why she was hooking up with Kim Jinhwan.

She didn't really even know where to begin explaining that one.

Feeling awkward and nervous under the harsh gaze of her elder, Soomi shifts uncomfortably in the leather chair which she sat across from him. The sunlight peeking through the large windows in the large office seemed to be mocking her as it beamed into her eyes, and she coughs a bit, trying to come up with the correct words to say.

"I'm sorry, there's just been some personal issues happening in my life, I haven't been feeling well mentally recently," she finally confesses, her eyes too afraid to meet those of her boss, "there's been a lot going on the last few years, and I just feel exhausted."

There's a notable, long silence that comes over the office of YG. Soomi only stares at her feet, far too worried of the expression that must be on his face. Was she about to get fired?

Until the sound of him clearing his throat is heard, and his deep voice cuts through the once eery silence, "You've been very busy since your debut, I understand you just need some time off. I'll cancel your current schedule and arrange for you to have some time to yourself." His words were thoughtful despite his voice still being as stern as ever. Either way, hearing such a thing caused her eyes to nearly bulge out of their sockets as she whipped her head back up to the CEO.

Surprise evident in her voice, she couldn't contain the overwhelming joy. "Really? Thank you so much!"

Though a rare occurrence, a small smile spreads over the lips of YG. "All you had to do was communicate, you're an important asset to this company, Soomi, take care of yourself."

Soomi rises to her feet, bowing a few times before she exits out of the room. A giddy expression was on her face, and she jumpily walks through the hallways of the studios. Many workers that had most likely seen her this morning - or just recently in usual - grew shocked at the sight of her so bright for once. Their eyes follow her as she bouncily jogs through the company.

Time to herself was all she had been wishing for what felt like a century now. At least, that was what she thought as she stepped out of the large doors of YG Entertainment, but now that she had rethought it, she was thinking all she'd really wanted was free time. Time to do whatever she wanted, free without having to worry about work, or what anyone around her was thinking about her. For once, Soomi felt like she was free to be herself as she inhales the outside air deeply, extending her arms beside her.

In that moment, as she pulls her car keys out of her bag and made her way to her Toyota, she had the perfect idea of how to celebrate.

It was like a sweet symphony, just the mere thought of eating food, that was driving them all mental.

he's running down the hall to his own bedroom as he screeches these truthful words, a rather ticked off soomi chasing close after him. she didn't know what it was going to take to finally get it through their heads - she wasn't dating kim jinhwan. it was like no matter how many times she said this, they all continuously insisted - like it was just to spite her.

only just as her small figure is quickly speeding past jinhwan's bedroom door to catch junhoe, his door had been opened. this revealed a tired jinhwan, his hair an unkempt mess on his head. he was in his boxers, and wearing nothing more than a white tank top - the material being rather thin, meaning his toned, baby soft skin was on display.

his face was bare, not a singular droplet of makeup on him, but somehow he still managed to have not one flaw. it blew her mind, and she felt herself gawking subconsciously as she met his confused eyes.

"soomi?" he blinks a few times, "what are you doing here?" his voice was raspy, and with the way he rubbed his eyes, it was clear he had just awoken from slumber.

she felt herself getting lost in just staring at him, so much that he had raised a hand, snapping his fingers in front of her face. at the sight of her like this, jinhwan seemed to finally have a good idea of what she was doing here. although they never did things like this this early, he had a feeling she was feeling rather different about it today.

a smirk spreads across his lips as he crosses his toned arms over his chest, his muscles popping out and causing her heart to pop in her chest once again, "you okay, sweetheart?"

his tone was mocking, and it caused her courage to be abruptly chunked back at her. snapping out of her gaze, she rolls her eyes, not another thought crossing her mind as she places both of her hands on his chest, feeling his chest muscles under her palms through the thin material. and even though it would've been easy for him to stop her, he only grinned deviously down at her as she pushed him back into his bedroom, closing the door with her foot.

at the fact she'd thought the complete wrong thing, he couldn't help but start laughing, "i'm not fucking you in the parking lot of the company, soomi."

her cheeks turn a light shade of pink, and she realizes what he had actually been doing when he begins to pull the hoodie over her head. wanting to quickly hide the blush, she grabs it from him and finishes pulling it down.

"boring," is all she says as she climbs off his lap and onto the middle seat since the cup holder was set back. after putting her seat belt on, she'd laid her head on his shoulder, yawning as she mutters, "let's go home then."

his bare shoulder was warm against her cheek. jinhwan taking off his hoodie left him in just his white tank top, much like the other day. this meant his tattoos were on full display, and she closed her eyes so she wasn't distracted by looking at them. because god knew it only made her crave him.

"cutie," she hears him mumble as he'd sped to the exit of the parking lot, chuckling to himself at how whipped he was for her.














07:00 | whipped cream

The end of the year award shows were coming up quicker than Soomi was expecting. With the days approaching at a scary speed, she only forced herself to work harder, even when she grew exhausted.

Weeks had passed, and with her waking up at 7 AM everyday and heading down to the studio to practice with her choreographer, she felt prepared to showcase her new song at MAMA, Melon, and the other shows that were scheduled. Although she had worked hard enough, and even begun the filming for the music video for her new single, this meant she had barely even spoken to Jinhwan. The boys were working on new music as well, as they were releasing a new song called I'm Ok. This meant they were also usually at the studios practicing, and their heavy schedules clashing against each other meant they hadn't said anything more than a mere 'hello' in those two weeks.

With all the blood, sweat, and tears she had spilt, she felt just like she had the last couple of years. Ever since her debut, Soomi had never even thought about a break. After all, being at the top was her dream, so she always wanted to constantly work towards it.

This in mind, you'd assume it would be easy for her to go back to the way she had always been. Hardworking was why the CEO always loved her so much along with her screaming talent. Never had she been distracted by anyone or anything, which was why it was always so easy for her to stay on task.

However, now that she genuinely thought about it, her slacking began when she met Jinhwan.

In a way, she didn't see that as a bad thing. Soomi had an undeniable liking towards him, one she couldn't seem to quite explain or put her finger on, or maybe she was just refusing to. But Jinhwan had pulled her out of a dark place. Even though she was successful, she'd been stressed with all the weights thrown on her shoulders. Without him, she would've only gotten worse. 

But she always grew to like being around him more than she should've. She liked the feeling of just being normal. The feeling that they were just normal idiots in their early twenties, making stupid decisions together without having to worry about what the next day brought. It was one she had never felt until she was with him, and the more she had experienced it, the more she craved it, she craved him.

Jinhwan ignited a flame inside of her. A flame of acceptance, of admiration, of love. There were so many things she liked about him. Other than loving her fans, she had never been sweet to anyone else. Soomi was always cold, she was always careless if it didn't have to do with her career.

But he changed that about her.

In that sense, she was thankful for Jinhwan. However, she knew that being around him for a mere second would only distract her from the tasks at hand more. She needed to make sure she had the choreo perfect, that she had the facial expressions perfect, and the live vocals. If everything wasn't precise, she feared in horror, she wouldn't be the number one anymore. 

Because deep down, even though she always acted as if she was strong, Soomi was scared and weak. She was vulnerable to the worries that formed in her head, and there were a lot of them.

Extending her arms to the air, a yawn leaves Soomi's lips as she tilts her head back, stretching her exhausted muscles. Yet another night of tireless practicing had passed, and she finally felt confident in the dance for her new song. 

Walking to the exit of her practice room, she grabs that same blue bag she always carried, slinging it over her shoulders. Running a hand through her damp hair from sweat, she flicks the light off as she leaves the room. For once, every thought in her head seemed to clear out, until she looked down at the bag she was carrying.

A vivid memory of Jinhwan shoots into her brain like a sleep dart. At once, it was as if someone had hypnotized her into such a sight, as she saw it again so clearly in her head. The way he was, the gentlemen act he claimed to go for. Of course, she was only joking with him when she said he wasn't. In reality, Jinhwan was probably the sweetest person she had ever met. Never had she seen someone be so selfless and thoughtful towards those around them. It was a strong quality and one of the many things she admired about him.

Just the thought of him and the magnificence he was made her want to text him, but she hurriedly beats the thought out of her head. I can't, she tells herself, no distractions. After all, the rehearsals for Melon started yesterday. I'll be seeing the boys there, anyway, she remembers, shaking her head in worry as she left the company that night.

The sound of her phone rapidly going off, not one but many times, was what woke Soomi up the next day. Her head was practically pounding from the annoying sound of the default ringtone, and she scurried out of her comfy duvet in search for the device, eager to stop the horrible tone. 

"I swear to god, I will murder whoever is calling me," she's mumbling when she looks to the alarm clock on her end table. It was five in the morning, and she was enjoying her beloved beauty sleep.

Due to the fact that her eyes were still half closed, she didn't even see who was calling when she slid her thumb across the screen to answer it. She also didn't notice it was a FaceTime call, meaning she nearly fell off her bed from shock when she saw a newly-awoke Jinhwan on her screen.

"Yah, Soomi-ah, you look like a mess, did you just wake up?" his raspy morning voice breaks through her skull like an avalanche, crushing all of her emotions and turning her into a hungry dog. 

Shaking the want away, she holds her phone with one hand as she falls back onto her comfy mattress, rubbing her eyes with the other. "Nani, it's five in the morning, of course I did," she rolls her eyes, not wasting a second to sass him.

Pouting from her rude tone, he wasn't too phased by it as he hums, "Mianhae, I just wanted to tell you I heard the teaser for your new song, it sounds so good! I can tell you've been working hard the last couple of weeks since we haven't gotten to see each other."

Still not fully awake, her head falls onto the soft pillow, making her words come out barely audible, "oh, thanks."

As soon as her face felt the featherlike fabric, she could feel the dreamland calling her once again. Jinhwan sees this, and begins clapping into the phone speaker as he calls, "Kim Soomi-ah, don't fall asleep!"

A whine of annoyance leaves her lips as she rolls onto her back, holding the phone above her. "I'm tired, I can't believe you woke me up for this."

"Why not? I missed you and I wanted you to know you're doing well."

"I'm literally going to see you in like five hours."

"Or you could see me right now when I come over."

"No," she's quick to snap at him, her eyes suddenly wide open as if she just heard something mind-blowing. 

He wasn't bothered by her stern voice, though. Through his phone camera, she could already see him getting out of bed. Soomi knew exactly what that meant, and her suspicion was confirmed further when he hums, "I'm on my way now."

Knowing there was no way he was going to listen to her telling him no for once, she groans, "ugh, wait, I'll just come to yours instead."

That seemed to of grabbed his attention, as he had stopped from digging through his closet to find some clothing to wear. Raising a brow, he asks, "why?"

Already climbing out of her own bed, she sighs, "because if I have to deal with your annoying ass, I at least want to eat Yunhyeong's cooking for breakfast."

It was an early morning in the iKON household. The boys mostly hardworking and only occasionally lazy, and today was one of those days where the determined, passionate side of them and their love for their job would come out. At around 7, the seven boys were awake and sitting in the kitchen while Yunhyeong was cooking when Soomi arrived.

The one who answered the door was Junhoe, who usually was never very thrilled to see her since she was around so often. If she was being honest, he was probably the one she got along the best with out of all the boys in the group. The both of them had the same sort of humor, and a knack for just messing around with everyone (then again so did the others,) but her and June had always connected in another way. The two of them showed their appreciation for each other through their negative comments and jokes.

However, the aura around him was different that day when he grinned at the sight of the small girl on their doorstep, "Soomi, you're alive."

"June-ya!" she screams like that of an obsessed fan girl, already beginning her child like attitude as she jumps forward to hug him, "it's been so long, you've already gotten taller!"

Although he reluctantly accepts her hug, he's chuckling as he shakes his head at her, "it's too early for this."

Frowning since he didn't play along like usual, she nods, "yeah, you're right," the rest of the boys had looked out into the living room to see what was going on. At the sight of her, they all seemed cheery, especially Jinhwan.

"Hi, Soomi, I didn't know you were coming over!" Donghyuck cries brightly as she walks over to hug him and the rest of the boys. 

They were all walking into the kitchen and taking their seats after she'd greeted everyone. Casually, she falls onto the booth, scooting in next to Jinhwan so there was enough room for Junhoe beside her as well. As she does so, she scooted so close to him her entire body was nearly one with his. It was an extremely unusual act out of her, and it had all the boys taking a double take.

Their minds wander back to nearly a month ago. We're just best friends, the words of the two of them repeated in their heads. Everyone at the table - except for possibly Soomi - knew Jinhwan had strong feelings for her. He never shut up about her, and that day when those words so normally slipped from her lips, they could tell his heart was demolished by hearing such.

But now that they were seeing what was right before them, the six of them exchange knowing glances. There was definitely a spark there.

"You got whipped cream on the corner of your mouth," Jinhwan isn't paying attention to the fact that everyone in the kitchen of the iKON dorm was watching the two of them like it was an intense drama as he giggles down at the girl beside him. 

Not really listening to his words, Soomi glances up to meet his humor tinted eyes, "huh?" However, she jumps when his face was abruptly right in front of hers, the proximity creating a tornado within her heart. She could practically feel the sweat forming on her forehead and the way she clenched her hands together under the table as he'd leaned it, kissing the corner of her mouth before ever so gently running his tongue across the corner, getting rid of the substance that had been there.

With her eyes bulging out of her sockets, she can only peer up at him, completely dumbstruck. The other members had witnessed the entire thing, and it was rather difficult for them to hold in their laughter at her blatant expression. Usually, Soomi was hard headed and stubborn. She refused to admit to her true feelings, and always liked to seem like nothing in the world could taint her untouchable attitude. But with the way Jihwan triumphantly grins down at her as if he had done the most wonderful deed, it was clear the table's were turning.

"Why are you gawking at me like that? Hurry and eat, rehearsals start soon," he hums to her as he goes back to eating his pancakes, snapping the shocked girl out of her daze.

Rubbing her temples, she shakes her head to try to rid herself of the tickling feeling creeping through her veins. This boy is something else.

Jinhwan tries not to show the obvious smirk on his face as he chews. For now, he had her right where he wanted her.




08:00 | bittersweet memories

Award show rehearsals were always hectic. Usually even more than the actual show itself, since it was the first time for some of the artists to be there after a year or at all. Nobody knew when they would be on, the arrangements, where to go at the right given second, and most importantly, who else would be there.

With the fact she had been one of the top winning artists for the last few years, Soomi was well known at every show. In fact, she was the top winning solo artist. With selling millions of albums globally, everyone - especially idol wise - knew who she was when she entered a room. She was never friends with many idols, as a lot of them didn't like her because of her success. As usual, she always shrugged it off, not her fault she was so talented.

At the new show tomorrow, she would be show casing her new single, How's This. It was a song that showed her carefree attitude she was so well known for, talking about how she likes to breathe and let go, live her life differently than the stereotypical idol. With an upbeat dance, she was sure her fans would react positively to her upcoming comeback.

Along with that, she was prepared for all the awards that were going to be announced that she was nominated for. She was even going to announce an award herself, one that was for boy groups. Actually, I'm pretty sure iKON are in the nominations as well.

She bows to the security guards that had escorted her to the doors of the backstage entrance of the enormous arena where Melon was held. There, they'd opened the door for her, and she hurries inside to the hectic area. Immediately, her eyes were met with the crowds and crowds of workers. Everyone, along with many recognizable idols, were in a rush to try to understand when they were coming on stage and what queue to look for.

With a sigh as she directs her eyes towards the stage, she recognizes one of the only friends she had practicing on stage for their performance. A smile finds it's way to her lips as she watches the girls of Blackpink. With their debut having had come a couple years ago, they were rising to fame quickly, about as fast as she had. The five of them got along well, and she was actually allowed to be around them.

Watching their rehearsal, she grows distracted for a while. She knew hers wasn't going to be around until towards the end of the show. They always saved the most shocking performances for that time. Then, at the end of the show, the grand prize would be announced, and the winning artist would give an encore stage.

Starting to bop her head along to the music the girls were performing, she saw a few idols she barely knew waving at her. Offering a grin and a wave back at them, she was pulled out of her trance when her phone furiously vibrates in the back pocket of her jeans.

Taking it out of her pocket, she has to hold her hand over the top of the phone to block out the lights so she could clearly read the text.

jinani:
come to our dressing room 

soomi:
y

jinani:
bc i wanna see you

soomi:
we saw each other like 2 hours ago

soomi:
jinhwan, you're so clingy

jinani:
if you knew how beautiful you were you would be too :)

jinani:
you're a little clingy too recently~
don't make me talk about the other day when I picked you up

shut up, don't

soomi:
give me a bit, i have to try to slip back there
 without anyone noticing

soomi:
you know it's dangerous :(

jinani:
we're dangerous. that's ok.

jinani:
be careful, baby <3


Her cheeks heat up just reading the name, and she quickly shoved her phone back in her pocket. Using her hands, she covers her face so people around her didn't see how angrily her cheeks were. Without another thought, she tries to think back to where the dressing rooms were, but how was she supposed to know where iKON's specifically was? It felt like there were over a million artists here.

Although she knew where the dressing room halls were, she didn't know which one they'd be down. However, thankfully she'd pulled out her phone just to ask him that question, only to see he'd already texted it to her.

Second hall, next to IU's and IZ*ONE's.

Blinking a few times as she mentally pictures the route, she types an okay, be there soon, before hitting the send button. She still had a while until it was her turn to rehearse, anyway. There was enough time to spare.

Deeply exhaling as if to prepare herself to go stealth mode, she puts her phone back in it's spot before scurrying through the crowds of people. As she does so, she keeps her head low in hopes no one pays much attention to her. If so, she was just going to act like she was going to her own dressing room anyway, since it was down the same hall.

"Excuse me, excuse me, mianhae," she's repeating the same words nearly every few seconds as she keeps accidentally bumping into people. In response, they'd brighten their eyes before bowing to her, offering her a hello. She noticed there were actually a lot of artists she didn't know, figuring they must be newbies to the business.

"Wah~, did you see that? Kim Soomi talked to me," one had whispered to another one of her members in exasperation, squealing like that of a child.

"She won top female artist every year since her debut, right?" another one had asked curiously.

"Yeah, she's so cool!" they'd all gushed to each other, and Soomi wanted to turn around and thank them, but she figured that'd be a little weird - and one of them might faint.

So, she only continued on her way. Finally, she was met with the many halls that each led down for what seemed like miles, lined with many dressing rooms for every artist there. Her eyes peered down each one, finding the second one, and she smiles victoriously to herself.

Just going to my own dressing room, she reminds herself, stepping out one foot to begin on her way. That was, until a boy who seemed to come out of the ceiling had stepped in front of her, preventing her from actually taking the step forward and scaring the living shit out of her.

"Yah!" she squeaks, a hand flying to her heart from the shock she had just been thrown into. Slowly, her green eyes make their way up the figure, and it takes her a moment to actually process who was standing in front of her.

The sight of the all too familiar face was enough for her to nearly belch on sight. Not because something was wrong with this particular person, but the astonishment of seeing them that brought upon her this certain feeling. In complete disbelief, she has to turn away, holding a hand to her head to try to calm her screaming emotions.

"Soomi-ah, you look like you just saw a ghost? Am I that scary?" the boy voices out, his now much taller height than her almost over bearing as he stepped a little closer, bending down to meet her eye level so he could peer at her.

His eyes were full of questions, full of things she knew he wanted to ask her. If she stayed around him any longer, if she spoke to him, she knew people would see. She knew he would see, he would come talk to her as well. 

She didn't have the strength to do that.

"Uh, I-," she can't seem to find words as she slowly backs away, the nerves she usually never had suddenly rising up inside of her like a wildfire. The memories began to shoot into her brain, the ones she had forced herself to push away and burn. They had come back to her as she felt her breathing grow irregular, everything was coming back to her. 

"I'll see you around, Jimin," she manages to voice out to stop herself from growing too emotional. I'm not like this anymore, she reminds herself harshly, I'm not that weak anymore.

Before he could say another word to convince her otherwise, she pushes past the old friend. Her feet are quick against the tiled floor, and she could hear the stunned boy call back to her in hope, "Soomi, wait, this isn't about-," but she didn't let herself hear the name.

She couldn't, not after all this time. How silly of her to think something like this wouldn't happen, of course they would be here, after all. What did she expect? 

For them to not approach her, she answered the question for herself mentally. Just meeting the eyes of him had brought it all back, all the glistening memories that turned bitter. Something so sweet had grown so sour, and it hurt her, even then, even now.

Pushing her hair out of her eyes as she continues running down the hall, she has to fight back the tears. I don't cry anymore, but sometimes, even with someone as strong-willed as Soomi, she couldn't hold it in.

Desperately, her eyes search for the familiar sign on one of the doors. Monsta X, Seventeen, Pentagon, she kept reading the names, growing more hopeful with each one. 

Until finally, there it was. 

iKON.

A breath of relief leaves her lips, and she rushes towards the door. Looking either sides of her, there was no sight of anyone around the halls. With one last exhale, she turns the door handle and runs into the room.

The seven boys were lounging around on the sofas set in the room. Their heads whip up in surprise to her, but unlike usual, it didn't disappear once they saw it was just her. No, they kept looking at her with wide eyes.

"Soomi, are you okay?" the concerned words were thrown at her from practically all of them at once, "what happened?!"

Blinking at them in wonder as to why they were asking, she raises a hand to feel under her eyes. She was crying, without even knowing.

"fuck," she mumbles under her breathe as she sniffles the pain away, dipping her head so her hair covered her face and using the back of her hand to wipe the tears away. She didn't want to be weak again.

Before she knew it, a certain boy was by her side. His hands make their way under her chin, where he forces to her look up so he could rid her of her tears himself. As he did so, she notices Jinhwan is already dressed, his makeup on as well, for his rehearsal. His light colored locks were styled to perfection, his dreamy eyes soft with worry as they stare down at her.

For a while, she wanted nothing more than to stare at him. He was so gorgeous to her, he was caring and loving. He was everything, and she had to tell herself that many times. Just looking up at his delicate expression, she felt safe. She felt okay again, just in his presence.

Until he finally uttered the words she had a feeling she was going to hear, "what's wrong, Soomi-ah?"

Letting out a deep breath, she tries to regain her composure. Forcing her courage to come back, she coughs a bit so her voice is back to normal, "nothing, it's really nothing, just an uh, an anxiety thing. I get a little nervous sometimes."

Every one of the boys was staring at her in distrust. A few of them exchange glances, a nervous look on their faces. It was clear they were all thinking the same thing, even Jinhwan had a small idea. After all, it was the only thing that would ever make someone so headstrong like Kim Soomi shed a tear. 

There wasn't a single person in the arena that didn't know about it.

And knowing who was there, they knew it made perfect since. 

A sigh leaves Jinhwan's lips as he feels nothing more than a bundle of mixed emotions piling up inside him. Shaking his head, he doesn't know what else to do as he wraps his arms around her, pulling her fragile body into his chest.

You'll be okay, Soomi.







09:00 | the scandal

They all offer her their bright smiles, showing their thanks for her words. Waving in return to her, she only watches as they all exit the dressing room.

A sigh leaves her lips as she watches them disappear into the hall. Now she just has to get out of here.

Running a hand through her hair, she waits a few minutes after they had left. The staff would most likely be coming back to their dressing room soon, so she knew she had to leave while it was still safe.

Walking to the door they had exited out of previously, she slowly turns the knob. Sticking her head out into the hall, she looks either way, seeing no one. This gives her the courage to casually walk out, a breath of relief leaving her lips as she breaks into a jog towards her own dressing room.

Pulling out the key she was given to it, she sticks it in the keyhole to unlock the door to her safe place. The only thing was, it was already unlocked.

Her eyes fall out of their sockets as she looks down at the handle, her mouth agape, completely dumbfounded. Who would've gotten into her room? She wonders in astonishment, backing up so she can double check the sign to make sure it was actually hers.

Sure enough, there was her name planted on the paper taped to the door. It was hers.

This only led her to wonder even more. Perhaps it was one of the staffs, but they don't usually leave the door unlocked. Also, there was no point for them to be here yet since there was still a while until her own rehearsal, so she didn't need to get into dressing yet.

Feeling a nervous pit form at the bottom of her stomach, she tried to think of what she was walking into as she turns the handle. Her feet feel heavy against the tiled floor, and slowly, she closes the door behind her. Pulling the hoodie off her head, she lets her locks fall down her back freely as she fully enters her dressing room.

Someone immediately rose from one of the sofas at the sight of her entrance. "Soomi," they speak her name in one breathe, their voice booming through her skull and throwing her into an instant trance. Her heart seems to come up her throat, and she feels her breathe hitch as she slowly turns, daring to meet their eyes.

No, her insides are screaming as she stares at the boy through the darkness of the sunglasses Bobby gave her, no, tell me this isn't happening.

Pulling off the sunglasses and the mask, she has to squint her eyes to make sure she wasn't seeing things.

He was really there.

Feeling like all of her emotions were bound to pour out of her at once, she felt her bottom lip quiver as she breathes out, "J-Jungkook?"

"I'm breaking up with you," he states again coldly, his eyes not meeting hers. Instead, they're staring ahead at a painting on the wall as he then warns, "so get the fuck out of my house."

The girl can only look up at him, gawking as a sign of disbelief and complete bewilderment. Her green eyes are glassy from the tears threatening to spill, and her jumbled mind tries to make up any sort of excuse for what was happening.

"Why? Is this just because of that?" she voices out her thoughts, and she knew he was aware of what she was talking about. How could he not be? It only happened hours ago. The events that occurred were so clear in her mind even though she tried to erase them, she thought everything would still be okay. 

Finally, when she still doesn't budge from where she's standing firmly on the carpeted floor, his doe like eyes find a way to hers. When they make eye contact, she searches for any sort of emotion on his face, scanning every inch of it. But there was nothing, he looked like a robot, only staring back at her emotionless.

"Leave," he repeats again, raising his voice and making it harsher.

Mouth agape, tears rush out of her eyes and begin to stream down her face just as quick as they fell. Everything in her heart, all the emotions she felt, were breaking out of her and falling around her like shattered glass. For once, after so long she'd laid her heart and soul out to someone, only for it to be violently torn apart so suddenly. She didn't understand, she couldn't understand.

"But why - just because of the anonymous letter sent to Dispatch?!" she cries out through her sobs, unable to control everything coming out of her as she falls to her knees.

Scoffing, the boy shakes his head in incredulity as he snaps, "you really don't get it do you? I sent the letter."

If she was stunned before, she definitely was now. Her eyes are wide as she looks back up to him from her spot on the ground, her voice cracking as she asks in bafflement, "what?!"

"I sent the letter to get rid of you," he explains fully, his face still showing no sign of emotion.

She couldn't believe it, not a single bit. With the way he'd previously looked at her, the way they kissed, the way they did everything together. It'd always been like their lives depend on each other, despite living the harsh idol life. As long as they had each other, they were happy. That's what she always thought because it was what he always told her, until this.

The entire time he was tired of her?

Each word flying from his lips was like a million daggers to her fragile heart. The tears are spilling in an eruption as she looks down at her hands, her green eyes falling onto a certain finger.

In whispers barely audible to the human ear, she whispers, "but you asked me to marry you..." her voice trails off as she stares down at the diamond ring on her left ring finger. It shone so brightly despite the dull atmosphere. The place she once grew so accustomed to because of the love it was covered in no longer felt like home as she watched the wet droplets fall onto the palms of her hand.

When she doesn't say anything, he sighs, holding her wrist and helping her to the elevator. The girl could seem to barely walk, and he hated to see her like this. Although he never mentioned it to her, he felt like maybe it was time to. Someone needed to inform her, to make her understand that that useless excuse of a guy wasn't worth her time. It was unhealthy for her to keep sitting around and ruining her life. She hadn't gotten fired from the company, but she sure was going to if she kept going on like this.

However, he just couldn't seem to form the right words in his head. Jinhwan knew her well, she was readable that way. Soomi was strong on the outside, but a feather on the inside. She was practically sensitive to everything, and he knew one wrong word would break her heart all over again.

If he did that, he'd never be able to live with himself.

"Jinani~, you're pretty cute, you know," her slurred words cut him off from his deep thoughts, and he looks down only to see her standing directly under him. Her green eyes are still visible through the darkness of the small space in the elevator, and although bloodshot, he still found them beautiful.

And even though kissing her would be a dream to him, he knew he couldn't. Soomi was healing, she was getting over a boy she loved. He wasn't going to take advantage of her or rush her through that process. Unlike Jungkook, he had respect for her well being. He just wanted her to be happy, he didn't care about himself.

She kept coming closer and closer to his face, the proximity decreasing as time passed. When their noses were nearly touching, their lips only centimeters apart, he knew it was time to stop her before he couldn't stop himself.

Using his pointer finger, he puts it on the tip of her nose and pushes her back. "You're drunk," he blatantly states.

Soomi pouts, "No, I'm Soomi."

Cute.

"Pabo," he mutters under his breath as the elevator dings. He decided to just take her to his apartment since he didn't know where hers even was, and he also didn't have the energy to try to get it out of her since she was so intoxicated. Turning back to the frowning girl, he offers his hand, "come on."

At the sight of this, she perks up like she was being offered candy. Together, they walked down the halls of the YG apartment complex, Jinhwan jingling his keys in the other hand.

"Jinani~, I think you're so special," she kept saying silly things as they went, "you make me forget about him, you're so much better~."

He felt his cheeks heating up, but it wasn't like she was even meaning these things. Shaking it off, he acted as if he wasn't listening to her musical words, stopping before the door of the iKON dorm.

The two of them enter, and he prayed for the boys to all be in their rooms asleep. Soomi is still humming from behind him as they walk inside, and she turns to close the door before looking around to the apartment.

On every wall was something about iKON. There were posters, albums, everything you could imagine was decorated in every corner. As if on queue as soon as she sees it, she's reminded of the newest song they had released.

He hadn't expected her to do anything once she saw them, though, until her yells fills the apartment as she screams, "BLING BLING~!"

"Yah!" he curses in a whisper, covering her mouth with his hands, "Be quiet, the others are asleep."

He also didn't want any of them to know she was here, but it was too late for that.

His nightmares were only further confirmed when a head peeks around from the kitchen, "Jinan brought a girl home-," Junhoe had been humorously making fun of this occurrence, but his mouth falls open when he sees her, "holy shit, is that Kim Soomi?!"

"Oh my god!" Soomi gasps as she gets out of Jinhwan's grip, walking towards the giant boy, "you're the super handsome one!" she points a finger at him knowingly, a satisfied smirk on her face.

Junhoe grins at this, not even noticing how drunk she was due to the compliment. Suddenly, someone else steps into view, "I'm afraid you're mistaken, that would be me."

She gawks at the sight of Yunhyeong. "Fuck~, I'm in a house of cute guys!"

Laughing at her, Junhoe took it into consideration as he looks to the dead inside Jinhwan, "Alright, so why is she shit faced out of her mind?"

The eldest only heaves out a sigh, mumbling, "Don't fucking ask," as he walks by, grabbing her arm on the way and dragging her towards his room.

"No, wait, I want to talk to him," she's whining in desperation, "he's cuter than you!"

"Soomi," Jinhwan pleads as they enter his bedroom, "please - shut up."

Pouting from his words, she falls onto his mattress, uttering an okay.

Silence engulfs the bedroom, and Soomi yawns as she lays her head onto the pillow. It seemed the alcohol was finally throwing her body into a desire for rest as she rubbed her eyes with her fists.

He had been rummaging in his closet to find her something to wear, when he hears a barely audible mumble from his mattress.

"I was just joking, I don't think anyone compares to you~," her voice seems to trail off into the atmosphere as her eyes are closed, but she still managed to utter her last words, "I really like you, Kim Jinhwan."

It's weird to think about, how if you exclude a minor thing from the past, your entire life could be drastically changed up until now. Even something as tiny as not saying hello to someone, or not picking something up, could be the mix between life and death. With the scary ways the world worked, this is what Soomi found herself thinking as she lets out a shaky sigh, her chin in the palm of her hand as her eyes fixate on the wall of her bedroom.

If whoever had blackmailed Jungkook hadn't, she would be married right now. She might not even still be an idol, fuck, she could've had a kid already. There were so many things that would've happened if such an obstacle hadn't occurred. Then, Jungkook wouldn't of done that to her, the confusion wouldn't of been created, she would still be with him.

But then, she wouldn't have met the boys, or Jinhwan.

All her life, she had heard the saying everything happens for a reason, and only now was she wondering if that was true.

"Jinhwan-hyung will come around, Soomi," Yunhyeong had been saying as he sits on her bed, along with the other boy who had been staying around at her apartment with her since after the rehearsals. They understood how it was all one big misunderstanding. Her emotions had gotten the best of her, and no doubt there was now a lot of things on her mind.

"He loves you," Yun had finished his statement with those three words.

Hearing that causes her to shift in her position, suddenly uncomfortable. He loves me, she repeats it in her head, and it sounded almost foreign the more she thought about it.

Noticing her distraught face, Junhoe wraps an arm around her shoulders in comfort. Thankful for him, a close lipped grin spreads over her face as she leans on his chest, deeply exhaling.

"I guess I just didn't want to be true to it," she finally admits, "I was scared of giving myself over to anyone else after that - but now I know all of it was forced, I just don't know how to feel."

In that moment, nothing could compare to how much she adored them. Nearly crying all over again this time out of gratitude to the two of them, she pulls Yunhyeong towards the two that were already hugging by his sleeve, forcing him to join in.

"Thank you both," she offers them as they all sit there on the edge of her bed, "nothing can explain how much I love you guys."

"We love you too, and so does Jinhwan, he'll come to his senses eventually and then you can tell him everything," Yun pats her back, and she nods in agreement, "I know every puzzle piece will fall into place, don't worry!"

She could only pray he was right.

With in the next couple of hours, Soomi and the two boys had spent their time in the living room of her dorm. Although it wasn't as big as the iKON one (since she was the only one living there versus seven grown boys,) it was still spacious and homey, so much that they found themselves liking it there. It was nice not having the noisy guys around, even though Junhoe was one of them, and they could just chill on the sofa, watching Soomi's new favorite TV show Gossip Girl.

"Soomi, aren't you part American?" Yunhyeong is casually starting a conversation as another episode ends. 

It was a question she hadn't heard in a long time, causing her to look up from her hand that was in the bowl of popcorn they were all sharing. Pursing her lips for a second as if in thought, she shifts in her seat, answering reluctantly, "uh, yeah."

She figured most people around already knew that. Most of her life she'd grown up there not knowing much of culture in Korea. She knew the language from speaking it in the house, but even then, they rarely spoke of formalities. 

This meant her family was still in the states, and the thought makes her nearly physically wince. She tried hard not to think of them, but it was hard not to when being asked such a question.

"Wah, so you understand what they're saying without the subtitles? I swear english is too hard," Junhoe is gasping as he looks completely flabbergasted from this information.

Nodding, she shrugs her shoulders as if it wasn't a big deal, "it's not as hard as you guys think, it's easier to learn than Korean."

"Is your family still there?"

She only nods, and a sympathetic look takes over Yun's expression. Wrapping an arm around her to give her a side hug, he soothes her obvious tainted emotions, "I'm sure they miss you, I hope you can see them soon."

"Me too," she hums, offering him a grin to show she was alright, "but also I don't want them to know about all this guy drama - I think my parents would murder me."

As if they would even care about her at this point, but Soomi keeps that smile on her face as if she had no problems with her family.

Yunhyeong starts giggling, and she eventually joins in, the two of them enjoying themselves in their own world. They'd been cracking jokes and having a good time, so much that they didn't notice Junhoe rising from his seat and wandering off to a shelf that was located near the corner of the living room. 

It was dark outside, and there were only a few lights in the room that illuminated it. None of them, however, were located in the corner where this shelf was. He has to use his phone to see what was on it, figuring it couldn't be anything that big of a deal to Soomi.

That is, until he sees a bright diamond ring on it, tucked into a velvet box next to a bundle of polaroids. At first, he's lost, thinking it was some sort of ring given to her by a family member. But when he notices the photos of her and Jungkook scattered around it, his mouth makes an 'o.'

Back when the scandal was released and then revealed to be true thanks to Dispatch, nobody ever really found out that they had been engaged. As far as anyone ever really knew, they just had a long relationship behind everyone's backs. That night when the reporter saw her ring, she had played it off like it was something else other than what it was.

And later on, Jungkook had denied it as well. Soomi had assumed he got rid of his own ring, and never spoke of it again to anyone.

She'd thought earlier, when telling the boys the truth about what went on to cause the scandal, that it would probably be a dire detail to tell them she was going to marry him. But a part of her was still scared to let that get out. Nobody knew, no one other than her and Jeon Jungkook himself.

So she hadn't told them. She just explained what everyone knew, how they had been together for so long and then filled them in on the shocking info she had just found out. The boys had been dumbfounded enough just hearing that part of the story, she could've only imagined what they would do if they knew they were engaged.

This was why a look of horror spreads over her face when she sees Junhoe holding the ring up in the air. Truthfully, there was no telling how much such a ring cost, it was why Yunhyeong had gawked when he saw the boy holding it as well.

"Put that down!" she snaps, as if a demon had jumped out of her. 

Surprised, he looks at her in confusion, "what is this?" 

Although Junhoe had already put most of the pieces together, he just didn't know if it was true or not. Yunhyeong seemed to get it right away as Soomi had rushed across the room to snatch the ring out of Junhoe's fingers, "is that an engagement ring?"

Feeling the anxiety creep up her spine, she frowns as she faces the both of them, the ring still clenched in her hand. Knowing she had no choice but to tell them now, she sighs, "yeah, uh, we got engaged the night before the scandal."

As soon as these words leave her lips, her eyes go to her feet, not wanting to look at them. Meanwhile, the two boys look as if they just got hit by an airplane as they could only stand there, their mouths wide open. It seemed to make even more sense to them why she had been so torn when it all went down, and even earlier.

They were engaged.

"Oh, I had no idea," Junhoe mumbles nervously, noticing her dull face, "I'm sorry," he bows apologetically.

After a moment, she turns on her heel to set the ring back down on the shelf. "It's okay, I honestly don't know why I still have it," she shares, walking back to the couch with him, "if I was smart I would've gotten rid of it by now."

"There's nothing wrong with still having it, Soomi," Yun shakes his head, putting a hand on her shoulder so she'll glance to him, "it reminds you of when you were happy, it's like a souvenir," he explains, before pointing a finger in acknowledgement, "plus, it sure looks like it's worth a hell of a lot of money."





14:00 | wrong confrontations

The 10th annual Melon Music Awards, also the first award show of the many that go on during the end of year. It was astonishing to believe it was already December, as it seemed like almost yesterday it'd just been a fall day in October. But the leaves had settled fully off the trees, and the weather was only getting colder in Seoul. 

Every attendee, and especially artists, were more hectic than ever during the month of December. After all, it was when all the award shows took place, it was when they had their chance to truly shine and be rewarded for their efforts. With three award shows happening in one month, with more in January, the artists who were performing for each show were especially nerve wrecked.

One of these happened to be Soomi. She had always worked hard for her career. The last couple of years since she hit it big, she'd been performing at every award show yearly. At this point, it was almost like a tradition. 

She understood there was a lot demanded of her with her being the top solo artist in the country. But with all the pressure, just like when she practically lost her mind with laziness from being so overworked, she felt dead inside.

"I think I'm worn for the day, gotta still have energy for the show, you know," she's saying to her back up dancers and the staffs with a fake smile. Thankfully, they nod in understanding. A breath of relief leaves her lips as she offers a goodbye, bowing politely before grabbing her bag.

It was early in the morning, and she had been scheduled to come practice the songs she would be performing tonight at the show. This was done every year by every artist who was scheduled to perform, so it was expected that the boys of iKON would also be at the company.

She had to be in tip top shape for the show tonight. If anything was wrong, her face might show it, and it would cause her fans to notice. She swore if she even didn't crack a smile at the right second, her fans practically jumped on her back. It was why she had to be careful and erase the thoughts from her mind.

Time, the word she had been using so much lately shoots back into her head, he needs time.

Jinhwan was never that kind of person. He was thoughtful, caring, passionate. 

Are you okay?" the sudden voice breaks her out of her racked emotions.

Surprised by the question, she slowly looked up at him, feeling like she had heard his voice from somewhere. At the sight of his face that was looking down at her, she nearly fell over in the elevator. If she hadn't been stunned then, she now felt like she was witnessing the coming of God from the sky.

She'd never felt so speechless under someone's gaze before. Despite the millions of people she had been in front of the thousands of acceptance speeches she'd given, nothing compared to the nauseous feeling that came up her stomach as she met his gaze.

It was then that she saw it. She saw the hurt he was hiding so deeply in his eyes. I did that to him.

Realizing she had been staring at him like he was an alien, she hurriedly speaks, although her voice was that of a mouse, "Soomi, nice to meet you - and uh, thank you."

He doesn't say anything, so she hesitantly goes on to admit, "I-I thought it would be best to give us both time, that's what I keep telling myself, but it's fate that brought us to run into each other, I know it. And - I can't stop thinking about you," she coughs a bit, feeling embarrassed about everything that was pouring out of her, "so please just talk to me, I miss you, Nani."

She expected him to come to his senses after her confession. She expected him to admit he was too harsh and that she at least deserved to have a right to explain to him what was going on. Soomi expected that soft sparkle to appear in his irresistible eyes, for that cute angel-like smile to spread over his kissable lips, and for his eyes to crinkle from the happiness he felt when he tells her I miss you too.

It envisioned in her mind so perfectly, she could see it happening in her head like it was playing out already before her on a television show.

Speaking as if they were already friends, he pouts, "Cheer up, Soomi-ah, following every day is a better tomorrow."

But it didn't happen.

In fact, Jinhwan didn't say a single word to her. In one breathe, he only ripped his hand out of her grip before spinning on his heel and walking the other way. He didn't even spare her another glance.

"Oh, Jinhwan-hyung, we were looking for you!" some of the boys appear around the corner, their eyes brightening once they find the boy they had been searching for.

"Soomi!" Junhoe calls out her name in excitement, waving his hands in a jazzy way, "Did you and uh, did you and Jinhwan talk?"

If he hadn't then, he knew by the shattered look on Soomi's face. The boys all frown, looking back to Jinhwan, but he didn't show a single sign of caring as he pushed passed his member, heading further down the hall and straight for the exit.

Knowing there was no way any of them were gonna get to him, the boys run up to her, having a feeling of how she was probably not doing to well after such a harsh confrontation. 

"It's okay, Soo, he'll come around," Donghyuk gives her a quick hug. The others mumbled noises and hums of agreement, hugging her after he had.

She forces a small smile, shaking her head dismissively, "I just never thought he'd treat me like that, he didn't even say anything."

"He's sensitive, that's for sure," Bobby hums.

"Just think about how big of a dick he's gonna feel like when he finds out everything."

Everyone slaps the maknae's arm in unison, as if it had been planned. He whines in fake pain as he flinches away from them, and Soomi couldn't help but giggle at their antics. 

She didn't know what she would do without all of them. Even though she hadn't done a very good thing to their hyung, they still were understanding to her. They still stood by her and treated her like their own family, and with the way they are now, they were her family.

he looks up from his phone that he'd been holding with his other hand, speaking casually, "i'm gonna drive you to the company."

she finds a melancholy feeling creeping inside of her veins as she slings her bag over her shoulders. he insisted on carrying it for her that day, and she had always been so confused by his sudden actions. In reality, he was just being a sweetheart, which was exactly what he was.

Jinhwan made her heart flutter in her chest. Even now as she thought about it, she had to hold a hand to her aching heart as she left her dorm, locking the door in the process.

"These are the songs you are set to perform tonight, yes?" her manager asks as he points down at a list, his fingers hovering over two of her new songs. Having had been out of breath due to the practice she just went through, she holds a hand to her forehead, looking to the list. 

Not having the energy to say any words, she nods with a forced smile. 

"I still feel like it would have been good to rehearse this one at least once," he's mumbling, shaking his head in obvious misunderstanding. She glances back down at the list, knowing exactly which one he was talking about.

She waves a hand in the air dismissively, "I don't need to, it's a very special track."

Although he still didn't seem to get it, he nodded. "If you say so, I trust in you, Soomi-ah."

Thankful for her manager's sweet words and understanding, Soomi bows in appreciation. "Thank you, Manager-nim."

"Of course," he holds his fist directly in front of his chest, doing a fighting sign before patting her shoulder, "so are you ready to win all the awards?" he hums enthusiastically, half joking and half pretty honestly.

Chuckling, she shrugs, pushing her hair out of her face. It was sticking to her because of the sweat, and finally, during their conversation the staffs had come back into the room to dab it away with cloths. She offered a smile when they also gave her water, immediately twisting the cap off like a mental patient and chugging it.

Her manager laughs as she does so since she looked absolutely ridiculous. Once the bottle was empty, she hands it back to the staff, who bow before excusing themselves once again. Looking back to her manager, she finally clears her throat, "I suppose so, but I don't think I'll win as much this year."

A gasp leaves his lips as if he was massively offended, "nonsense, your new song is going to be a hit, I can already tell!"

Shaking her head, the smile doesn't leave her lips for a second as she hesitantly agrees, "I just hope you're right."

"I am, don't worry so much," he reassures her. The conversation dies down after this, and only then did she notice most of the staffs were leaving the room. Her backup dancers seemed to already headed out, and some of the workers were standing at the entrance of the dance practice studio they both stood in.

One of them waved their hands to grab their attention, "it's time to head to the arena, Ms. Soomi-ah!"

"See you there, manager-nim!" she yells as she runs out of the room. 

The halls of YG Entertainment were crowded. Lots of artists were walking, along with all their staffs and workers that were carrying things like makeup bags and outfit changes. It was hectic as everyone was chattering loudly about the events that were bound to happen, such as who was performing what and who was winning what award.

Her green eyes trail along the artists and staff, searching for the familiar boys she wished to speak to. While her eyes search, it isn't long until they land on a certain group of boys. A giggle leaves her lips when she looks at the height difference, her eyes landing on Jinhwan.

However, just seeing the way he was dressed, the way he was that gorgeous, was enough to cause her to frown.

Just when she's about to start pushing past people like a crazy woman, screaming their names, someone puts a hand on her shoulder.

This scared the shit out of her as she had been preparing herself. Jumping, she holds a hand to her heart as she tries to think of who would be bothering her. It wasn't like many people liked her really, or they were too scared to talk to her in the first place.

But everything seemed to make sense when she sees the four girls standing there beside her, walking at the same pace. Bright smiles are planted over their faces when they see she noticed them, and they all squeal in excitement, "Soomi-ah~!"

"Oh my god!" Soomi screeches so loud a lot of people in the hall turned around to look at her in confusion, including Jinhwan himself, "I haven't seen you guys in so long!" 

The five of them gather in a large hug, nearly crying tears of joy because it really has been that long. It was an emotional time for them as they pull away, still walking together out the doors of the company. 

"Yeah, you're so busy being successful," Rose jokes as she slaps her shoulder in a playful manner.

Soomi wrinkles her nose, shaking her head vigorously in disagreement, "oh please, and you guys aren't?!"

They shrug, knowing they couldn't dismiss it. In reality, Blackpink had exploded practically everywhere. They were now the top girl group in the world. 

Lisa wraps an arm around her shoulder as they walk, "maybe, but just think how unstoppable we'd be if you debuted with us."

Soomi chuckles, "I think it'd be too much for people to handle."

Back in 2015, when the original plan for Blackpink's first name - PinkPunk - was created, it involved Soomi in the mix. Unlike the other trainees who trained with the four girls who left early on, Soomi trained with them throughout their days. The five of them had been an inseparable team, but the CEO had taken her out of the project, saying that she would be better off as a solo artist. She never really got why, and the girls had been bummed out since they all were so close. But she never got to debut with them, and eventually she came out as a female artist alone, and the girls debuted as Blackpink.

Although she didn't mind how her career itself turned out, she couldn't help but wonder what it could be like if she was with them.

Jennie points a finger in agreement, "now that is true," she wraps an arm around Soomi too, and the other girls join in. Together, they walk with their arms wrapped around each other. Lisa kept making jokes about how Soomi would probably be the main rapper, and Soomi kept denying it, fake rapping and purposely sounding horrible.

It had everyone of them in fits of laughter as they board the vehicles. For once, Soomi found herself smiling not because of a boy, but because she had friends. She had real friends who she had missed through out everything in her life. 

She felt like she was part of Blackpink then. Like she had debuted with the girls. It was a pleasant feeling - one she wished she had always.

17:00 | home

The award show was almost over. Thankfully, after what felt like so long of just sitting there and watching artists and awards be given away, Soomi would be able to go home soon. The thought of laying on her bed was the only thing keeping her alive right then. She'd won five awards in total that night, and she was beyond joyous to her beloved fans. But even then, a part of her was missing. She didn't know what that eye contact had meant between her and Jinhwan, or if it really meant anything. He seemed so determined to not show her any sign of emotion, and she had finally given up when he didn't react much to the song that was obviously written about him. Did he just suddenly not care?

She couldn't help but feel like he was overreacting, just in the slightest. The two of them weren't even together officially, but yet he was acting like she had done some sort of drastic sin when all it was was a heat of the moment kiss.

Did he really not care about her now because of that? Could she really be blamed for her actions? The two of them had never truly been open about their real feelings for each other, but was that her fault?

As the night went on and she kept thinking about his lack of reaction, these are the sorts of questions that pounded their way into her skull. She was so distraught about it all, that she didn't even pay attention to the boys of iKON the rest of the night. So much that she didn't notice the certain boy on her mind that was finally trying to get her attention.

Every year, boy groups were usually given it, since they were where most of the popularity was. This is why she showed basically no interest in announcer, instead distracting herself by entertaining fans that were waving and filming her by making funny faces.

Finally, the other boys were giving short thank you's. Just when she thought they were about to finish so that the ending ceremony could begin, Jungkook looks to his hyung's as if asking permission. Everyone nods at him, and he hesitantly stepped up to the mic, straightening it with his hand.

Soomi's gawking at the stage, and Jungkook catches her dumbfounded look, shooting nothing more than a wink her way. She couldn't process it, what was he trying to do?!

"I had really strict parents, they basically held a gun to me and my siblings heads with everything we did," she looks to him again to see he was looking at her weirdly from her words, so she hurries to explain further, "I mean they were controlling. it was like, sure, you always want the best for your kids - but they never let us make any decisions on our own. They were rich, well known business folk in the area, so if anyone in the family ever made a wrong move it was death for you. You'd be all over the media, and it would blow up right in your face and your parents faces."

There's a look of astonishment on Jinhwan's face as he can only seem to mumble, "I never thought you'd come from a family like that."

She shrugs, looking up to the stars as she goes on, "Well, yeah, it's not something I like to share with anyone in Korea. Long story short, we'll just say I did something that didn't only blow up in my parents' faces, it pretty much exploded. They breathed down my neck so hard after that, so when I turned 18 I just decided to leave, I just couldn't take it anymore," she sighs, shaking her head at the memory, "I called up my old family here in Korea, and I bought a cheap ticket and just - left," her eyes grow dull at the thought as she admits all her mistakes, "changed my number, got an ID with a Korean name instead, and asked my relatives to never give them any information about me."

"What?" Jinhwan gawks, "but you're - you don't live with your relatives anymore. You never spoke to your family back in the States? Don't you want to see them, don't you think they want to see you?!" he wasn't speaking in anyway rudely, but just out of complete concern. 

A bitter laugh leaves the lips of the idol star, and she takes the hood of her jacket off her head to fix her hair, "No, trust me, if my parents wanted to find me, they could very easily."

Sympathetically, his face falls as he mutters, "what about your siblings?"

"I don't know," she shrugs, "I'm sure they're fine. It's not like I don't miss them, but it's not my business to barge into their lives, and it's not like I can now, anyway."

His mouth slightly agape as he tries to find the words to say, something to convince her she should try to see them. Jinhwan loved his family, he kept them so close to his dear heart that it broke it just hearing about this, about how Soomi's life really was. 

It was then, that he really got it. He understood her trust issues didn't come from the scandal, they came from a lifetime of betrayal and hurt. She was treated like a dog by her own parents, and as he listened to her go on to explain how they neglected and treated her in such ways for such silly things, like when she wouldn't get an A on a school assignment, he couldn't understand it any better.

Because where someone comes from has an impact on who they become.

With a sigh, Jinhwan wraps an arm around her shoulder, startling her at first. Pulling her into him, her head lands on his chest as they walk, their footsteps in sync. The wind blows against them, creating goosebumps up their skin and leaving a chill against their spines. But either way, in that moment as he assured her he would always be there, that he loved her, they still felt warm. They felt warm with the presence for each other, and the love between them that was spiraling through the air from their hearts.
