"Oh, I almost forgot to tell you!" she suddenly gasps after popping another fry in her mouth, shifting in her seat as Jinhwan looks up to her with curious eyes, "It's about the song."

He raises a brow in question, "the song, as in the one we're making together?"

Soomi knew he was referring to her and not only him but all the boys of iKON, it was why she couldn't hide the devious grin that spreads over her lips as she boasts, "no, this song is just going to be us!"

Blinking a few times, he stared at her in disbelief. "What, really?!"

Nodding vigorously, she continues eating her McDonald's fries, "Yeah, me and Hanbin are already working on the song, and we were thinking it would be perfect for just the two of us, and then we can all just do another song together," she explains what her and Hanbin had spoken about regarding the song only hours ago, "course, we still have to run it by the CEO but, surely he won't mind!"

Chuckling in astonishment, Jinhwan reaches over the table to grab her hand. Intertwining their fingers, he squeezes it as he gushes, "that's great, I'm so excited."

"Me too, you think we could finish it in time for MAMA?"

Jinhwan furrows his brows as he grasps her words, "huh? Are you suggested we could perform it there?"

Without a second thought, Soomi shrugs casually, "yeah, why not?"

When she looks back up to him from her food again, he's staring down at her like she was a mental patient. Feeling a bit nervous under his gaze, she opens her mouth to speak, when he beat her to it. With words dripping of concern, he sighs, "Soomi-ah, are you alright?"

"Better than ever," she only hums, wondering what he seemed so bothered about, "why?"

"I don't know," his voice is a mumble as he thinks hard about it, still holding onto her hand, "it's just - you used to be so worried about getting caught, and now it's like you want to seize the world together," he laughs from his choice of words, a smile hinting it's way on his lips as he confesses, "I'm just really happy we're like this, I don't want it to change, I don't want you to change."

Before she can say anything, he raises the back of her hand to his lips, leaving a lingering kiss there. Soomi's eyes remain on his brown orbs as it falls back to the table, and she purses her lips for a second.

"Well, we still have to be careful but I'm not as focused on it as I used to be," she offers an explanation hesitantly, "It was all I used to think about, was 'what if someone sees,' or 'what if someone finds out,' and it kept me from being as happy as I could be. In reality, I just want to be with you, and it's not that I don't care about my career, but I love you, and I'm not afraid to show that."

Jinhwan was smiling from ear to ear, his heart pumping out of his chest as he rises to his feet. Walking over to her side of the table, he pulled her up, causing her to gently hit his chest as he returns the bright grin. 

Nothing could explain the bliss he felt exploding within him as he leaned down to connect his lips with hers. He kissed her not once, but twice, pulling away for only a millisecond in between each one. With lips that were so soft, so sweet, he never wanted to stop. He never wanted to stop showing her how much she really meant to him.

That was, until he realized they were still standing in a fast food restaurant. 

"Let's go," he whispers as they finally pulled away, his hand finding hers again. 

Soomi only nods in agreement, smiling giddily to herself as they make their way out of the nearly empty restaurant. 

The cold night air fans their skin as they leave, and her eyes wander to the skies. The stars were still out, mockingly shining down upon them, and she couldn't help but gawk up at the wonders of the dark sky above. Even the moon was such a sight, and it had always been one of her favorite activities just to stare at it.

With the only sound being the slight blowing of the wind through the trees, Soomi and Jinhwan began their walk home. After walking through the park for hours, getting food and ice cream from a cheap fast food place, and going into WalMart to buy useless things they didn't need, she felt normal.

She felt like she was a teenager again, doing whatever she wanted and whenever she pleased. Like this was just something she did so casually with the boy she loved. For once, it didn't feel like she was a celebrity. It didn't feel like she had to go to the company in the morning, or sing in front of millions of people.

It didn't feel like she had to live her life according to pointless rules in a book, no dating, no clubbing, no freedom. She just felt normal, like there was nothing to hide in her life.

And even though it wasn't true, it felt like it was. 

Soomi wished that feeling would never leave. 





22:00 | new rules

"Hanbin-ah!" she boasts in excitement, extending her arms out to show her enthusiasm to the boy. Usually she would have greeted him with a hug, and he knew this well, but instead she keeps her distance feet away from him, only bowing politely and forming a kind smile on her lips. 

Staring at her weirdly, he bows in return hesitantly, "Soomi," he hums out her name in a greeting, "what's up with the attitude?"

Soomi peered up at him from her small height like he was insane, shaking her head in disappointment that he didn't get it. When he only continues to look at her in wonder, she scoffs, "Silly, we're at the company, I can't seem all friendly with you."

Indeed, the two of them were standing in front of YG Entertainment at exactly 10 in the morning. With only getting a few hours of sleep, she felt like her body was bound to shut down any minute, but she remembers her and Hanbin had plans to meet up at the studio - but she thought she meant his studio. This was why it was rather difficult for her to comprehend when he called her to inform he meant the company studio, meaning they would be out in view for anyone to see. 

At the fact that anyone could do something as simple as snap a photo when she got too close to the idol and practically end her career, to say she was horrified was an understatement.

But when she meets his gaze, there's a humorous glint in his eyes. In disbelief, she realizes he must know something she didn't, otherwise he would be acting the same way. Through his child like chuckles, he offers an explanation, "it's okay, the CEO actually scheduled for us to be in the studio, so we can work on that song."

"I got a call this morning, apparently he's open to us working together, dropping the whole 'we can't be seen with each other' rule if there even was one."

She could hardly believe it.

"No way!" she screams accidentally, unable to contain her joy. Moving her hands and body in spastic ways as they walk in the building, she whisper yells to Hanbin, gaining them some weird looks from her behavior, "I can finally be around you guys without getting in trouble - this is a miracle!"

Laughing at her reaction, he nods in agreement, "Yeah, CEO-nim really believes we can make something great together, so I'm hoping to live up to those expectations."

Hanbin only shakes his head sympathetically, "No but I don't think he would say no, he seems to be in a good mood recently."

Letting out a breathe, she hums as the elevator dings and they exit towards the studio, "Yeah, it's a relief. Guess we can only hope for the best."

The next few hours, you'd find the two of them working their asses off. Hanbin had previously been under an impression Soomi was a bit lazy, and she liked to talk more than work. However, that was only because he had never seen her when she was working. The truth was, if Kim Soomi set her mind on something, it always got done. And this song was something she definitely had her mind set on, she wasn't planning to rest until it was done.

And being that Hanbin was a hard worker himself, especially when it came to making songs, you'd imagine they would be the ultimate team. But the unfortunate part was that both of them were a little too used to working by themselves, so much that Soomi got distracted with in her own thoughts and ideas and forgot to even tell him what she was doing.

The clock had struck 1 PM, and they had most of the song lyrics for her and Jinhwan's song finished - but most of them had been written by her. Hanbin was the one working on the music itself, and the two were having a rather hard time agreeing on certain melodies and rhythms, when it was as if a light bulb had popped above her head.

Diverting her eyes from the computer screen he was focusing on, mixing different beats together to try to form something, she put a hand to her forehead and stared down at the paper where the lyrics were. Maybe if I did that, and then that, she formatted things in her mind, like she always did when she was producing and writing. 

Pursing her lips, it came to her. As she spins in the roll-y chair back towards Hanbin, his phone suddenly went off in his back pocket, snapping him out of his serious daze.

She watches as he pulls it out in confusion, and his eyes seemed to brighten like the sun when he set sight on whoever it was. Soomi wasn't dumb, and she rose a brow as he looked back up to her with pleading eyes, "Answer it, I need to use the computer anyway."

He mouths a thank you to her, before walking out of the recording and writing studio. Soomi only watches him leave, offering him a grin and a thumbs up. 

Once he's gone, a breath of relief leaves her lips. In only a second, she fell into the chair, scooting forward so she was close enough to see the computer screen.

"Time to make a song," she mutters to herself, leaning in to begin. This was getting done today if it was the last thing she did.

She could only hope so.



23:00 | number one

"Good job today, you two!" her manager was clapping, a proud look plastered on his expression as she leaves the recording room. Soomi felt like her soul had left her body from working literally from morning to night on the song, not taking more than a couple minutes of a break, but now that it was finished - she felt good, more than good. That feeling only increased when she sees the wide smile on Jinhwan's lips, as he rises from one of the booth seats in the room and walked closer to her.

From the way their eyes met, his irises burning into her green orbs, she could feel the tension in the air. She wanted to hug him, and do even more than that when her lips momentarily flicker to his, they looked so soft. 

"Thank you, but most of it was really Soomi," she jumped in surprise from the feeling of a hand on her shoulder. The familiar cologne filled her nostrils only a second later, and she felt a lump form in her throat when she looked to her side, noticing the close proximity suddenly between them. 

However, Jinhwan wasn't looking at her, but to the staff that sat around the computer, and her manager that was standing before them. She swore behind the angelic smile on his lips that there was a smirk, was he aware of how she was feeling right now? How was he having such an easy time? Soomi wanted nothing more than to release all the stress she'd been feeling after working all day, he could tell, couldn't he?

With wide eyes, her head jerks to watch the staff that are still gathered around the computer. That's our song? she asked herself mentally, not seeming to believe that the perfect sound that was filling the room was really theirs.

But soon, the gorgeous voice of Kim Jinhwan had filled her ears, and it was enough for her to realize it. She wrote those lyrics, this really was their song. Soomi hadn't expected it to sound so good, they really did work wonders.

24:00 | apartment rendezvous

Exhaling deeply, she clicks the post button, watching as the app loads and prepares the photo. Only a second later had it been thrown out into the world, and she purses her lips, tapping on the notifications bar and refreshing. Her green eyes are met with already thousands of likes and comments, and her heart felt full of joy as she scrolled through them.

This was the basis of her morning. Soomi and Jinhwan's song had been sent to the CEO, who would check over the song and report back to her manager and staff, that would report back to her and Jinhwan. If he ended up liking it, they'd hopefully be able to perform it at the next award show coming up with in the next couple of weeks, right before Christmas. 

However, it was obviously going to take more than just a couple of hours for their boss to run over the new song and decipher how he felt about it. This meant all she felt like doing was waiting, as her mind was too full to even think about writing another song.

Although to her dismay, there was still work to do. Even though her and Jinhwan's song was done, there was still an expected collaboration with her and all the boys of iKON together. They were going to the studio to write today, and they'd even come into Jinhwan's room - where she spent the night - asking if she was coming along. The boys had been confused when she declined, but they reluctantly left without her.

Even Jinhwan had gone, as he had been talking about wanting to really get into songwriting himself lately. She admired his desire, he was already talented enough as it was, but he always kept striving to better himself. It was one of the many things she adored about Kim Jinhwan.

On the other hand, since they were all gone to the company, this left her in the dorm of iKON by herself. She was wearing one of Jinhwan's hoodies, and the only thing keeping her sane as she sat on the edge of his bed, dangling her legs back and forth, was the scent of that cologne she loved radiating off the material. 

A dull sigh leaves her lips as she replies to more comments from her fans. It seemed that people really were liking her new single and even the other side track she performed that was meant for Jinhwan (though thankfully no one knew that.) Everyone was very hyped about her new EP, and she was thrilled for the support. 

Even with what Jungkook had pulled at Melon, people weren't giving her any hate. Sure, she always got a few rude comments here and there, but she expected for them to be as bad as they were when the scandal happened.

But they weren't. As she scrolled, she even saw a few comments talking about how great her and Jungkook would look together. There ended up being more than she planned for regarding her ex fiance, and it was enough to make her stop reading them. I don't think I can see anymore of that.

The last thing she wanted to think about was him.

Sighing, she's about to logout of Instagram itself, when her phone refreshes her feed, and a new post appears.

        

gnani___: recording. big surprise coming to u soon ikonics!

She never knew it was possible for someone's heart to clench so much from seeing one person. Holding a hand to her temples that seemed to be exploding, she could only gawk down at it in disbelief. He was something else.

There were thousands and thousands of comments under the post only minutes later as she was still staring at it. She chuckled as she read some of them, people really were passionate about their love for him - and she found it completely understandable.

As she stared at it, she realized she missed him, even though it had only been around four hours since the guys left. Although she had been planning to just wait at the guys' dorm all day, she was starting to get a bit bored.

I'll just go to my apartment and watch Gossip Girl, she thinks to herself. It was as if a giant light bulb appeared above her head as she climbs out of Jinhwan's bed, gathering her things. Since there weren't many things of hers around - other than her clothes on the floor from last night - it wasn't a huge task to throw it all in that blue bag of hers.

28:00 | rooftop secrets

"Yah, Chim," she calls out his name through the wind, reaching out a hand to touch his shoulder to grab his attention fully. Under the darkening sky at the night grew closer, his eyes find a way to meet hers. Throughout all her naivety, she grins up at him, her green irises glistening under the small amount of sunlight that was peeking through the clouds, "thank you, this was such a great day."

As she says this, she stands and grins up at him for a minute. When he doesn't say anything immediately, her eyes trail away, and her small body turns towards the view they were surrounded by. In awe, they rake over every detail of New York City, taking in everything that was truly before her after so long. 

This was her home, she thought, completely astonished. The city didn't look the same in her eyes as it once had. It was full of so many memories, so many terrible occurrences, and all of her stupid decisions she would never get over. But yet, as her eyes shine at all the city lights that glow in so many different colors, she saw hope in such a city, a city she was born it.

"It was the greatest day," her best friend's words finally cut through the wind. It blew so angrily every couple of minutes, as if it was screaming at someone, at them. What it was trying to say? She'd never know.

Her eyes merely glance up to the boy who was now standing beside her, resting his hands on the railing around the rooftop of the building they stood upon. Jimin's eyes watch over the entire city they were surrounded by, until they find a way to look back to her.

Thinking back to the stories of her family here, how she came to Korea, he frowned as he exhaled, "of course they are, and I know they think about you all the time."

She only makes a hmph sound in reply, and he pouts as he glances down to her gloomy expression, "I told you we could go visit them before we leave."

Sighing, she lifts her head to stand up straight, shaking her head, "I know, I know, I just - I don't think I'm ready to see them," she admits in a small voice, turning away.

He nods in understanding as he walks to where she was, feet away from the railing now, "I get it, it's okay," he reassures her with a grin, "but whenever you are, they'll be happy to see you," he informs her sternly, before adding, "and I'll be right here with you."

"Thank you," is all she can find to say to him. 

Words could never add up to how much she adored her best friend. If she hadn't ran into him that day, if she hadn't ever met him, she wouldn't even be where she was standing right now. 

Jimin only waves a hand in dismissal, turning away from her to pull out his cell phone. She watched curiously as he ignored the texts that were on his screen to slide it over to the camera app, switching it to the front view. 

"Smile, so we can remember this moment forever," he instructs as he holds up the phone in front of both of them.

Giddily, she tried to push her hair out of her face as she prepared to take the photo. With glistening eyes, she peered up at the camera that he was holding, and then, even without the photo, she knew she'd remember that moment forever.

Soomi only nods, turning to look at the view one last time. She didn't know then when she would be back here, and she squinted her eyes to peer out in the direction her family lived. To think they were only around half an hour away, just a short drive. But she wasn't ready to see them, she still felt like they weren't happy with her. As far as she knew, they forgot she even existed.

Thinking back to her best friend's reassuring words, she abruptly spins on her heel and steps forward without looking. A squeak leaves her lips when she runs into Jimin, who had been casually waiting for her. 

His eyes widen in shock when he looks down to her, only to see she was already looking up at him. Their eyes meet for a while, faces only centimeters apart. A lump forms in his throat as he tried to fight the urge that was desperately eating his insides.

What surprised him was the state of shock Soomi seemed to be in as she opened her mouth and then closed it again, not seeming to know what words to say or if she should say anything. Her eyes look in every which way that isn't at him, and she bit her lip, not understanding why this sudden proximity was suddenly so awkward between them.

Jimin, on the other hand, knew exactly why. The tension he was feeling between them was almost over bearing, and he didn't know what to do about it.

After this night, she was going to be engaged to Jungkook. They were going to get married. He'd never get that chance he wished for all this time.

"Jimin," she breathes out, suddenly lost for words as his face was inching closer to her own.

But before she could say anything else, there was a slight push against the nape of her neck. Her eyes bulge out of surprise when she sees his eyes flutter shut, feeling the softest lips against her own. 

He kissed her, and the tingling feeling of his pillow lips remained on her own as he pulled away after a second. Jimin's eyes were widened themselves as he seemed to process what he just did, stuttering out in a nervous mess, "S-Shit, Soomi, I'm sorry, I wasn't thinking-," she only looked at him, thinking about everything that just happened.

A part of her wasn't thinking either, to tell the truth.

"I know that was wrong of me, I'm sorry," he kept ranting on, apologizing more times than she could manage to count.

Just when he opens his mouth to speak again, she steps forward to enclose the space between them again. Cupping his cheeks, she abruptly kisses him again, and he didn't waste any time to return her efforts. Their lips moved in a melody with each other, shooting a euphoric spark through the veins and pumping off of their adrenaline.

He kissed her like he was running out of air and she was his oxygen source. As if everything fell into place, her hands go behind him to tangle in his soft hair, and he bit her bottom lip through the kiss, gaining entrance to her mouth. 

Never did she think her best friend was such a good kisser.

And never did she think she'd be kissing him in the first place.

"Fuck," she curses loudly as they pull away, her hand going to cover her mouth as she realizes what she just did.

Jimin tried not to smirk, partly being satisfied and feeling like at least he had to live with. But the part of him that cared for her as his best friend felt horrible. Running a hand through his hair, he tries to calm her, "Soomi, Soomi, calm down, it's okay."

"It's not okay!" she squeaks, her hands on the sides of her head, fingers tangling in her brown locks as she paces around the rooftop frantically, "I'm a horrible person!"

Sighing, Jimin reaches out to grab her wrist, stopping her from walking around like a crazy person. Reluctantly, she meets his stern eyes with a pout. 

"Stop, this is between us, okay? I won't tell anyone," he assures her, "you love Jungkook, and that's all that matters right now."

There was more meaning to his words than Soomi was aware of. Due to the stressed thoughts in her mind though, she hadn't noticed it as she nods hesitantly, agreeing, "okay, you're right. I love Jungkook," she raises her voice confidently, forcing a grin on her lips.

Soomi turns way to walk towards the exit since it was time to go meet him wherever he may be. Her best friend only watched her go as she took a piece of him with her, thinking back to those three words she just said that broke his heart in two.

She loves Jungkook, not you.

No sex would make it better this time, nothing could make her ignore the fact this person had access to her own home, all of her things, at their own will. There was no telling how many times they'd come into her house when she was by herself.

Just the thought makes her cry harder. Jinhwan hugs her so tight, she could almost suffocate from his grip on her. But then, it was just what she needed to slightly make it all better, even if it was momentarily.

He kept apologizing and saying everything would be okay. Really, she wished she could believe him. Jinhwan was such a sweetheart, she loved him more than she could begin to explain. This happening was only making her realize that more. But for once, his words felt rather empty to her.

What could either of them really do? How could they find them?

"I'm so scared, Jinani," she whined into his chest, voice a muffled mess of emotion. She knew he didn't really know the full story, he didn't know why.

"Soo-," he begins to say, but she only lets the first syllable leave his mouth before she speaks again.

Standing up straight so he could hear her clearly, his arms don't leave her as she sighs, "i-it's been going on ever since I was engaged, that's when it started," Jinhwan seems to have a knowing look on his face. She remembered then, the boys and him knew this much from the fight they had that time. "Jungkook had been the one getting the threats, it's why he broke it off, and I didn't receive anything since then," her voice trembles every few words, but she forces herself to go on, to tell the truth, "the first one was when I was FaceTiming you, and I told you I had to go so suddenly and we didn't talk for a while. The night I invited you over and Jungkook was there, that's why. He was the only one who knew about it, I didn't want to worry anyone else so I called him because he seemed like the only one I could talk to."

He opens his mouth to say something again, but she doesn't let him. "Then just not long ago, I started getting texts. The first thing was a note stabbed into my door with a knife, but now they have my number, and they've been in my apartment. I'm trying to focus on the shows coming up and our music but I can't when this person is threatening my life," she's in tears again, barely being able to speak as they wash down her cheeks, "t-they could've killed me already if they wanted to, I-I could be dead-," unable to hear anymore, Jinhwan abruptly shushes her, pulling her into his chest again.

"Stop," he demands harshly, "don't ever say that."

Balling his shirt in her fists, she pulls him closer as if it was even possible. Her nostrils inhale his scent what seems like a million times, afraid it was the last time she would be able to.

"I'm sorry," she muttered after a few seconds, "I just - I don't know what to do."

"Firstly," Jinhwan sighs, "you aren't living in that apartment anymore."

Soomi stands up again to peer up at Jinhwan in confusion. "What?" she breathes out in question, even though it wasn't hard to comprehend what he was hinting at.

"I'm taking you back with the guys, and we're packing your bags," he had no intention of giving her any sort of choice as he informs her of this, "you're moving in with us, and I will never let you leave my sight," his stern tone pings her heart as he stares down at her with glowing eyes, "and if you get another text, tell me immediately, alright?"

She was happy with his demands. The last thing Soomi wanted was to ever be alone anymore.

"Okay," she mumbled, not having the strength to say anything else.

Jinhwan doesn't either for a long while, he only hugs her as tight as he could manage. His chin rests atop her head from the fact he still managed to be taller than her, and he pauses the action to leave a lingering kiss on her forehead.

"We don't have to go back there tonight," he says after a while, "we can go tomorrow or whenever you're ready."

She only nods in his chest, not wanting to speak. All she wanted in that moment was him, not sexually, but just him. Soomi just wanted his presence, to feel the up and down heaving of his chest as he breathes against her, to know he was there with her and not going anywhere. The feeling that Jinhwan was holding her was enough to make her feel stronger.

"We can go tonight."

He hadn't expected to hear her say such. Jinhwan thought it would be a while before she felt up to going back to the apartment.

"Are you sure?"

"Yeah."

Pursing his lips, there was no point in questioning her, "okay, if you're ready."

"Yeah," she repeats, finally pulling out of his everlasting embrace. His hand finds it's way back to hers, and she feels calmed by the warmth of it in her own. Facing the door to the iKON dance studio, she uses her free hand to fix her messy hair that was falling in her face, "let's go."

Jinhwan only mutters an okay, leading the way with her behind him. Neither of them had any intention of letting their hands go, even though they were about to walk openly in the hallway of YG studios. He meant it when he said he was never letting her leave his sight, especially now that he knew what was going on.

"Soomi-ah," he suddenly halts his movement just as he's about to open the door. Soomi nearly crashes into his chest from not expecting him to do such, and her green eyes inquisitively meet his own.

"I love you, don't forget that, okay?"

She burst into laughter at his blatantly honest response. Holding a hand over her mouth, it takes her a few minutes to falter her hysterics. Hanbin starts laughing, too, after a moment. "What, am I wrong? He's too bossy."

"Yah," she's still laughing every few seconds, "I'm gonna tell him you said that."

Hanbin shrugs it off, "Hey, go ahead."

That heartfelt conversation she had with Hanbin had been her fuel for waking up the next morning. The last few days until MAMA had been irregularly quiet for her regarding the psycho, and it was nice to just be able to focus on work. She hadn't even really heard from Jungkook.

This was why she thought MAMA would go smoothly. For once, she could have a nice, peaceful award show where she gets to have fun showcasing new songs and just enjoy spending time with her fans.

And crazily enough, it did.

Her and Jinhwan's performance went extremely great. Everyone received it well, all the fans couldn't stop screaming during every second from how excited they were to see the idols together. The fact they were 'friends' was now out in the open, and the song they sang had everyone jumping around. 

Not to mention the choreography, that was simple and cute. There were fans that already seemed to have it down just from seeing it one time. The happy response made her excited to perform it on shows. After all, there was no better feeling than people enjoying something you wrote and produced. It was the solemn reason she liked doing what she did.

Winning countless awards for top female artist, top solo artist, and top choreography, was something she was used to. Soomi usually won these awards every single year. It was no different this time, especially after she released her newest song. Like per usual with her music, it was well received by the public.

And like everyone expected, despite her scandals, she remained on top. 

The song she did with the boys of iKON had the crowd in even more screams. It was bad enough when they said her and Jinhwan did a song, but seeing her come on stage with all seven of them, she didn't think she'd ever heard louder screaming in her life thus far.

Although she was exhausted as she walked backstage, she could finally say that she was happy. It was a word she hadn't gotten to use in a long time because of all the stress she had been feeling. But Soomi felt great, the award show was going great, and it was already almost over. What more could go wrong now?

She's just turning down the hall where her dressing room was, when the sound of fast footsteps cause her to turn. It wasn't fast enough, though, because soon, someone appears right before her.

"Soomi-ah!" the screaming voices didn't stop there, and before she knew it, there were four screeching girls surrounding her.

"I can't believe you got to do a song with iKON!" Lisa had been crying.

"It was so good," Jisoo is reassuring her as she hugs her from the side, "you're so talented!"

"Seriously, that duet with Jinhwan, I got chills," Rose is gushing as she holds a hand to her heart, acting as if she was in some sort of pain.

She couldn't help but smile from ear to ear as all the girls offer her a hug, boasting about how much they loved her performances. They were both under the same company, meaning they knew how strict their CEO usually was. The girls were seriously shocked that he really let her collab with them.

"I remember he doesn't even let us near them most of the time," they're saying in disbelief at how insane the rules tended to be at the company. Soomi knew well of them, and as she thought about it, they really were right - it was nuts how he was allowing her to be friends with iKON so casually.

"Yah, it's cause CEO-nim really loves Soomi," Jennie informs the others, and she looks to the girl who was trying to insist that that wasn't true, "then again, who doesn't?" she gushes, wrapping an arm around her shoulders and pulling her in for another hug.

The rookie idols around them were looking at the five girls like they were witnessing some sort of Gods. It must've been quite a sight to them, as they probably didn't imagine some of the biggest stars in Korea acted this childish.

"Hey," Soomi is whining as Jennie is practically hugging the life out of her. The girls are all in fits of laughter at the sight of the unconditional love the girl was giving her. Despite her cries, Jennie didn't seem to have much of an intention to stop squeezing her. "Jennie Kim, you make me think you're into me or something."

Even that comment didn't make her let go. She only hugged her tighter. "I don't know, you're pretty cute," the girls all burst into more hysterics when she says this. Soomi's mouth falls open out of surprise, it was the last thing she thought she would hear out of her.

Finally, she lets go of her, and she couldn't help but stand in astonishment. "I really never thought I'd hear those words," she's telling them, still shaking her head as she tries to process if that was what Jennie said or not.

"ooh, that would really shock the world," Rose is humming, "imagine Dispatch releasing news of you two being together instead of something like Soomi and Jungkook."

There's a tint of pink on her cheeks from the thought. Soomi raises her hands to cover her face when Jennie gently elbows her side, "hey, I'm down if your down."

Their jokes were driving her crazy.

"Hajima~," she's whining like a child, still covering her face with her hands so her words were just barely audible.

"Alright, alright," Lisa sighs after they all have one last good laugh, "we're done."

The three girls look to Jennie, who was still standing beside Soomi with her lips pursed. She seemed to be thinking seriously about something. At the sight, Jisoo raises a brow, "Not so sure about Jen, though, I think she's really considering hitting on you, Soo."

"Yah!" Jennie cries out upon hearing what she said, "cut it out~."

Just when another joking session is bound to begin, there's a presence coming up behind Soomi that causes all four of the girls to pause. Their eyes widen a bit in surprise at seeing them, and they exchange looks. They guessed they really shouldn't be surprised anymore. It should've been obvious that Soomi had close relations with those boys ever since that day at the hospital, after all, Soomi had told them that herself. But still, it was a crazy story to think about.

They couldn't help but wonder if she was something more with one of them. Soomi would never quite tell them that part.

Confused at why they all went dead silent, Soomi herself is about to turn to see what was going on, when someone suddenly grabs onto her shoulders, yelling boo directly in her ear. It was something she definitely hadn't been expecting, as she jumps, holding a hand to her heart.

Spinning to face the culprit, there's an unimpressed look on her face despite the grin on theirs. "Idiot, what's wrong with you?!" she pouts, reaching out to slap his arm like it would even slightly affect him.

June is giggling like a little kid, flinching away from her hits. "Nothing, I just wanted to find you, our set just ended and everyone is celebrating back in the dressing room," he explains to her, that bright smile never leaving his lips once. Seeing Junhoe's smile was contagious, it always had been. It was big and lively and just made you want to - well - smile. 

The girls are all whispering to each other behind her, and she purses her lips as she turns to them. Junhoe notices they were there, as he seemed to of forgot, and offers a quick bow and a wave to his fellow company-mates, "hi, nice to see you~"

They offer greetings and bows in return since they weren't really well acquainted with each other like they were with Soomi. She sighs as she looks between the two friends of hers, "I guess I'll come, you guys don't mind do you?" she asks the girls, who quickly wave it off.

"It's all good, we have to go on stage soon," Jisoo reassures her with a kind grin, giving her one last hug to congratulate her on everything.

"See you later, Soo, don't do anything scandalous in the dressing rooms," Lisa is telling her as she hugs her like Jisoo previously had.

Her face grows red at the sound of what she'd said. "Scandalous," she repeats the word blankly, "with who?"

The girl shakes her head is dismay, "you know who," she tries to nonchalantly motion to Junhoe, who was busy looking at something else that he actually didn't notice.

Realizing what exactly she was thinking, Soomi nearly falls on the ground from bewilderment. "Wait, no, it's not like that-," she's insisting, but the girl just shakes her head, already turning to walk away.

"Bye Soomi, you better call me so we can go on a date sometime," Jennie was still up with her jokes - or maybe they weren't jokes - as she hugs her like the others had.

They all wave goodbye to each other until the girls disappear down the halls to their own room. With a sigh, she turns back to Junhoe, who was giving her a weird look she couldn't decipher.

"What?" she asks him in confusion.

"Are you two-timing Jinhwan with Jennie?"

She couldn't help but laugh at what he said. Junhoe was obviously joking, as he starts laughing himself seconds later.

"Shut up," is all she says, grabbing his arm and dragging him down the hall. "I need to change and get my stuff out of my dressing room real quick, then we can go to you guys'," she informs June of her plan as they go down the hall where her's was.

He skips a bit to catch up to her quick walking pace, "mkay, no problem."

Soomi let's out a breath of relief as they walk down the seemingly quiet hallway. The show was practically over, all that was left was the closing stage. Nothing bad had happened, no drama had gone on, everything was fine. It was a normal, perfect award show.

Finally, something was going right. And with that, she couldn't help but smile.











41:00 | ancient pictures


"It won't take me long," she assures Junhoe, who only nods, distracted by something on his phone. He leans against the wall to wait for her, and she takes out her key to unlock the door to her dressing room. 

Twisting the key in the lock, the click sounds, and she turns the knob, pushing the door open. The outfit she wore for her stage was rather tight, and she was more than ready to get out of it, even if it meant she had to get back into the short dress she was wearing for the award show itself. Honestly, the dress was more comfortable.

Plus, it was pretty fun to wear heels. They made her taller than Jinhwan usually, and then she got to tease him with the others.

She was already unzipping the back of the outfit, which was some sort of one piece. Just when it's halfway down, does she walk into the main room of her dressing room. Like one would assume, it was completely empty, not a soul in sight. All that was located inside of it was things the staff left behind and her things like her purse and her phone.

A yawn leaves her lips as she unzips the rest of the outfit, just when she's about to take it off, her head looks up to the large mirror that covered the entire wall of the room. It was a big mirror, one that you could see your entire body in and showed every flaw if you had any. There were giant, circular bulbs that surrounded the outside lines of it, and it was a fancy, extremely expensive mirror she always liked to look into.

But not when it was cracked. 

Pieces of the mirror cover the ground she stood on. The wall was so big, that it was cracked on either side, like someone had thrown something at it or hit it with something. There's fear written all over Soomi's face, and she was in so much petrification she didn't know if she should scream or run - or both.

The worst part - was the sight of the word written on the mirror in some sort of red substance. 

Whore.

That sick feeling, the nauseating feeling that she was going to puke up everything wrong she had ever done, one she hadn't felt in the last few days. The peace that had finally come back to her that she missed so dearly, it was gone in the blink of an eye.

Tears rush to her eyes, and she didn't even care about the fact her outfit was completely unzipped in the back. She ran out of the room like a mad man, trying to wipe away the tears before they messed up her makeup. There were too many emotions in her head, so many that she didn't even know what to say when she swings open the door in a rush.

The slam of the door against the wall causes Junhoe to look up, a curious look on his face. Once his eyes land on the freaked out, crying girl, concern builds inside of those brown irises. He's stepping forward quickly, immediately assuming the worst and grabbing her like a protective mother.

"Yah, yah, what's wrong? Are you okay?" he's demanding as Soomi only grabs onto the jacket he was wearing, burying her face in his chest.

Worried someone might see them, he gently moves with her back into her dressing room hall. Closing the door, he clicks the lock before turning back to her. She was a mess of trembles, holding her arms and breathing heavily, like something traumatizing had happened to her.

He frowns at the sight. The one time everything seemed to be going well for her. All he knew to do was pull her into another hug.

They stood there, embracing, until she finally felt her breathing go back to normal. 

"June-ya," she mutters, her voice shaking with each word, "l-look inside the dressing room."

He didn't get what could possibly be wrong with her room, but there was only one way for him to find out. Pulling out of the hug, Soomi grabs onto his hand and follows him as he walked deeper into her room. He never really went into anyone else's dressing room before, but it was similar to how their's looked. 

His brown eyes rake across everything. It all seemed fine at first, and he wasn't sure what could have caused her to have some sort of breakdown - that was, until he saw the mirror.

"What the fuck?" he's gasping in awe. His hand falls from hers due to the fact he lets go so he could walk up to the mess that was created on the floor. Junhoe narrows his eyes at the sight, feeling the anger build up inside of him at the fact this awful person was still at it. How could they do things like this?

"I c-can't believe they can even get into my dressing room," she's mumbling from where she still stands, holding a hand to her aching head from what was going on, "how? How can no one ever see them?!"

Junhoe didn't know what to tell her. He was too busy leaning forward, inspecting whatever the word was written with on the mirror. A part of him wanted to touch it to try to figure it out, but from the fact it was red, he had a bad feeling about it.

"I'm sorry, Soomi-ah," he sighs as he turns back to her, "we should probably call your manager and tell him about this, I think it's getting too far."

"I can't tell him everything, though, he'll ask where I'm living and it's not like I can say I'm staying with you guys," she shook her head, "I'll just say someone broke in and trashed my room."

There's still a dull look on his face from realizing she was right, "alright, tell him that."

Soomi tried her best not to really freak out about the whole dressing room thing. The word they wrote on the mirror or the fact they broke it wasn't what had her nearly on the verge of a heart attack. It was more of the fact this person somehow got into her dressing room in the first place, they had access to her things, somehow even at shows like MAMA. No matter how many times she wracked her brain about it, looking for some sort of explanation to how they could manage it, nothing made sense. How could someone manage to have access to her dressing room, all without anyone thinking it was odd? Not to mention her apartment she was horrified to live in now. Something was weird about it, she just couldn't find any pieces to the puzzle.

"It's okay, Soo," Junhoe had been trying to comfort her as they walk in the boys dressing room minutes later, "at least they don't know where you're staying at now, and we're all here to protect you."

All she had the energy to do in response was send him a smile of thanks. Really, she was beyond grateful for Junhoe. Even though in the beginning she found him annoying, he grew on her over time. Him and his dumb sense of humor was comforting in the weirdest times, and he always knew how to make her laugh when she needed something to cheer her up. But even with his playful aura, when time came to be, he could be as serious as anyone when he needed to be. No one paid attention, not even the two of them themselves, but Soomi and Junhoe had become close over the last year, and especially the last several months.

Although Jimin was back in her life, she still saw him as one of her best friends.

The sound of the two entering the main part of the dressing room causes all the boys to look up. They'd been engaged in a serious talk about what kind of alcohol they wanted to buy to drink back at the dorm to celebrate their awards. There was a sense of joy in the atmosphere, and she didn't want to ruin it.

Soomi tries to force a smile on her face, but it was far too late when their eyes all land on her glassy eyes and distressed expression. 

As if he had some sort of teleportation skill, Jinhwan was suddenly before her. "What's wrong? What happened?" when he notices she doesn't look much for talking, he'd immediately looked to the tall boy that stood beside her.

He made sure to exchange a glance with Soo first to make sure it was okay to tell them. When she only nods to him, he clears his throat to explain, "someone broke into Soomi's dressing room."

All of the boys seemed to rise to their feet from the outrage they felt. "What?!" a few of them say in unison, shock written all over their faces.

Just like Soomi, it made zero sense to them. 

"No fucking way," Hanbin mutters, "how the hell is that even possible?"

"This is getting too far," Donghyuk shakes his head in worry for his dear friend, repeating the same phrase Junhoe had said back in her room.

Meanwhile, Jinhwan couldn't be more angry. Soomi had stepped forward to wrap her arms around his torso, and he allowed her to bury her face in his chest as he held her head with one hand, messing with her hair. The other was secured around the small of her back, and he was too busy trying to comfort her while attempting to figure out how this person could manage something like that. He was beyond angry at that point, the more he thought about it. It really was getting too out of hand, so much he was considering contacting the authorities and hiring extra security around their building or something.

He didn't know what to do. What could he do to catch this person? Whatever it required, he'd figure it out and wouldn't hesitate to deliver. He'd kill them when he finds them.

As if he couldn't get any more upset upon the news, Junhoe finally adds the rest of the story, "yeah, they broke her mirror and wrote uh - a not so very nice insult on it in some sort of red liquid."

Everyone got goosebumps from the words. "Was it blood?" Bobby is the first to ask, but Junhoe only shrugs.

"I think we should really tell someone," Yun was saying, "this is too much, I'm worried about Soomi's safety."

"We can ask the security here, maybe there's camera footage of whoever went into her room," Chanwoo suggests, and everyone perks up at the idea.

After a talk about it, they all agreed to head to the security team of MAMA after the final stage. It would be happening soon, and all they had to do was go stand out on the stage for one final goodbye to everyone who came tonight. Soomi couldn't help but recall the last goodbye stage she was on, which was at Melon when Jinhwan was mad at her. 

Jeez, she thought, how times had changed. At least she had him on her side now for good, even if she wasn't sure about her decision just yet. 

Jinhwan and Jungkook, the two that surprisingly hadn't been on her mind as much as usual. With the entire thing going on, she really hadn't had time to worry about who she really fell for.

Snuggling her face further into his chest, the warmth of Jinhwan was something she craved, she could confirm that for sure. The feeling of being in the same room as him was enough to make her heart leap, and she lets out a deep breathe, inhaling that cologne he always wore. 

We'll find them, she tries to tell herself, this will be over and I'll be able to live normally.

It wasn't like one could be so sure, but what more could she say to cheer herself up?

"iKON, we need you on stage in five," one of the staffs knock on the door, calling to them. 

They'd all rose to their feet, and Hanbin assured the staff they would be there in time for the final stage. 

"Guess we better get going," he'd hummed, being the first to walk to the door.

The rest follow him into the narrow hall, everyone making sure their wardrobe was okay even though their stylists just did that previously. Soomi actually hadn't seen her stylist since they were located in her dressing room. She figured she should probably head back there to check with them, especially because they probably saw what happened to the mirror. It was now or never for her to tell her manager not about the entire situation, but just that someone broke into her room. He would probably go check the camera's himself, which would save them the effort after the stage.

"I have to go back to my room," she's whispers to Jinhwan as they're walking into the main hall, and he'd nodded down to her.

Sending him a smile, she figured he would let go of her hand and go with his own members to the stage. Soomi was going to offer to meet him on the outside so they could go on by each other.

But he didn't let go, he only walked next to her as she turns to head the way her own room was.

Although it surprised her, she decided not to say anything. The feeling of his hand in hers sent butterflies throughout her entire body, so much that she didn't care who saw. 

Except for the staffs of YG, she did care if they saw. It was why once they neared her room, their hands fell out of each other's.

"I'll wait out here," he'd told her, and she only responds with a nod.

Just as she's walking in the hall of her own room, closing the door behind her, her phone buzzes in her pocket.

It's probably one of the guys asking if Jinhwan went with me, she assumes, pulling it out quickly to tell them he did.

42:00 | gallant boys



"Thanks to everyone for attending the 2019 MAMA, we hope to see you all next year!" the hosts had been cheerily yelling into the mics over the screaming of the fans in the crowds. There were so many lights and bright faces, and the sight of the signs they held up with her name made Soomi feel better momentarily. It warmed her heart to be in the presence of her beloved fans, they were the only reason any of her dreams had ever come true, after all.

All the artists are waving to their fans, shouting goodbyes to them. It was finally the end of the show, and she lets out a deep breathe as she rushes off the stage, making sure to wave before she does so. Her head was beginning to feel rather light again, and she was worried she might faint like she did at Melon.

I can't, she tells herself harshly. Even though there were so many people here for her, she didn't want to cause anyone anymore trouble. This was why she hadn't told Jinhwan about the new text message from the psycho.

Well, and the fact it would require her explaining what happened on that rooftop. If she had to do that, it would mean she had to admit to Jinhwan everything about her and Jimin. Did her best friend have feelings for her? She'd wondered it ever since that day, and never did she really know the answer. But then again, why else would they have kissed on that rooftop? 

Everyone got caught up in the moment sometimes. That was what she'd been telling herself was the reason for years. Even then, she never truly knew, and she never asked either since they grew apart. 

Now that the two were on talking terms again, she just didn't have the guts to bring that up. As far as she knew, Jimin probably didn't even remember. So she pushed it to the back of her mind despite the memory being so clear, it didn't matter. She didn't think she would have any reason to ever bring it up again.

Until now, now she had no choice but to talk to Jimin. The only person who had that photo was him, so how could this person ever had managed to get it? How did they know about what happened? It only caused her fear to grow more, and she holds a hand to her head as she pushes through the crowds of staffs and idols.

It might not have been the best time to have the talk with him then, but she didn't know when would be a good time. Soomi didn't have the energy to visit their dorm right now, and she needed to inform him about this now. 

Desperately, her green eyes rake over all the crowds of people in search for her best friend. No sign of Jimin was seen anywhere - or any member of BTS - and the hopeless feeling was surfacing in her veins again. Her only lead then was the fact there was a small chance her manager would find something on the camera footage he said he would search after she told him about her room incident. 

Somehow, she would catch this person that was bringing all of this stress and pain upon her. One way or another, she would find a way to find them.

Finally, after what felt like years of searching for them, she sees the seven boys walking off stage in a group. They all looked rather upbeat, probably because they got to see their fans and won some awards that night. Not that she was one to enjoy bursting bubbles, but she didn't have a choice.

The only one out of the seven that wasn't looking great was Jungkook. He kept running a hand through his hair, a habit he did when he was in deep contemplation, and he would stare off into space as the others chatted amongst themselves. She wondered how he'd been the last few days, as she really meant it when she said she hadn't heard from him much. Something about him looked different, it seemed like he was growing his hair out a lot more than usual. It was a good look on him, no doubt.

Jinhwan couldn't know what happened on that rooftop because then he would suspect her best friend having feelings for Jimin. And she didn't want him to dislike him since they seemed to get along fine unlike him and Jungkook. Not to mention, it could make him feel distrustworthy towards her since she'd done that while she was with someone. She felt like she had already tainted with that enough.

And God knew Jungkook couldn't know. She'd cheated on him the night he asked her to marry him. They hadn't been engaged when her and Jimin were on that rooftop, yet, and it was just a kiss, but either way, cheating was cheating. With how competitive and protective he was, if he found out Jimin had kissed his girlfriend at the time that he was still in love with, something bad would go down that she couldn't bare to be responsible for.

Just when Soomi opens her mouth to call to Jimin, who was too distracted talking to Hoseok to notice her presence since she was still rather far from them, a force on her wrist causes her to halt in her jogging towards the group.

"Yah!" she's crying out in annoyance, spinning around to face whoever dared to do such a thing.

The eyes of Kim Jinhwan pierce into her own, and the upset expression was wiped off her face the minute she met them. He stared into her soul for a second, before trailing towards where she seemed to be in such a rush to get to.

"where you going to see Jungkook?" the blatant question leaves his lips rather monotone. 

She hadn't expected Jinhwan to come out nowhere. For once, he wasn't actually on her mind since she was so determined to inform Jimin about the text messages. Meeting those eyes of his, any words she had been planning to say seconds ago seemed to disappear. Even though it wasn't long ago that they had that talk about how he understood she still had some sort of feelings for Jungkook, and that he would have to live with it and wouldn't get mad, Jinhwan looked mad. Maybe a part of him forgot about that talk overall, and she guessed he wasn't wrong for that. They were supposed to of taken a break from each other after that sort of conversation, but Soomi ran right back to him like she always did. 

So, could she really blame him for seeming a little upset? No.

"I'm not going to see him," his grip on her wrist seemed to release from how tight it had been. Realizing others might be watching, he lets go of her fully as a breathe leaves his lips and he comes back to his senses. "I was going to go talk to Jimin about what happened," she explains before jealous Jinhwan got any other ideas.

Although she was worried he was going to ask more questions, he only lets out a sigh, "oh, alright, do you want me to come with you?"

Soomi couldn't help but giggle at his question. Jinhwan really was cute, you couldn't deny it, but he was scary when he wanted to be as well. His duality was something she adored deeply about him, so much she could melt into the ground as she met those chocolate eyes of his. 

"No, I'm fine," she assures him, "I'll meet you in the dressing room after I do this and then go see my manager and we can leave, okay?"

The caramel haired boy only nods, and that bright grin of his finds it's way back onto his lips. His eyes were flickering from meeting her own green irises, to her lips, in a cycle that was driving her insane as she shifts her weight from foot to foot in the middle of the backstage for MAMA. 

"I wish I could kiss you right now," he'd blurted with a pout, and Soomi felt her cheeks heating up from the sound of those words leaving his mouth around so many people.

Thankfully, people were too busy rushing past them and trying to get their stuff together to head home after the show, that no one had the time to pay attention to the two idols. Still, she felt the need to raise her hands over her tinted cheeks so Jinhwan couldn't make fun of her.

"Shut up, go to your room," she whines, turning away from the giggling boy who still noticed the effect he had on her.

Jinhwan hesitantly made his way back to the boys dressing room, turning back and glancing at Soomi every now and then. He wasn't trying to be creepy, or clingy, he just meant it when he said he'd watch her like a hawk. The thought that that stalker could still be somewhere around here, watching them, had his senses on their best behavior. How could he take his eyes off her in such a time?

At this thought, he abruptly turns and heads down a different hallway.

"Chim!" she's calling, breaking into a jog to catch up with the seven boys that were all walking together towards their dressing room, "Jimin-ah!"

Since it wasn't as loud in the hallways, her shouts were loud enough for them to hear her. All of the boys turn to see the petite girl running up to them, eyes wide with worry as she looks to her best friend.

"Soo, nice to see you!" Namjoon greets, and the others followed suit as well.

"Your new songs were so good," Hoseok was telling her as she accepted his side hug, "you and Jinhwan are no joke."

She offers them a small smile, "thanks, guys."

Jungkook's eyes were piercing holes into her soul, so much that she was too afraid to meet his eyes. Instead, she clears her throat as she looks to Jimin, "I really need to talk to you."

The other boys were wondrous about what it could possibly be about. They knew about small parts of what was going on, but she didn't really know if either Jungkook or Jimin ever told them the full story. One thing they did know, however, was the tension that was always between the two members anytime it came to Soomi. 

It was obvious Jungkook wasn't happy she was just asking to talk to him. He'd already been on edge because of that competitive personality of his. Jungkook hated seeing her perform with the Jinhwan guy, after all he couldn't stand him. What he hated even more was how happy she looked with him, how bright her eyes would shine, and how big she'd smile. 

Sure, he was glad she found happiness. But he loved her, so strongly it was beginning to tear him apart. Seeing her happy with someone else was a nightmare to Jungkook.

"He invited himself," Jimin explains blatantly, motioning to the maknae who sent him a glare. Ignoring the look from Jungkook, he sighs as he admits, "I just wanted to make sure you were okay."

Soomi is about to speak up and assure them that she was alright thanks to her lovely friends, when all of the words she had in her head seemed to fly out her ears, somewhere far away from her brain. Jungkook had stepped forward to enclose the space between them. The mere foot was nonexistent as he wrapped his arms around her, not pulling her into him but just hugging her. It wasn't a tight hug like he usually did, squeezing the life out of her, but was just a comforting embrace.

"Jimin told me, I'm sorry, Mi," his heartfelt words shocked Jimin as much as they did her. She could only gawk at him like he was some sort of alien as he pulled away from the hug.

It was seriously out of place to see someone like Jungkook say something so selfless. They knew he was clingy when it came to Soomi, meaning the last thing they thought he would tell her was something like that. He expressed his clear disliking towards Jinhwan on the way to Ilsan-ri, and Jimin rolls her eyes from the fact he was probably just doing it to suck up to her.

Really, there was no way he could feel the slightest bit of bad about something happening to Jinhwan. If anything, he felt bad about the fact it made Soomi so sad. Nobody liked seeing her in such a state, and they all wanted to rid her off the stress this person was causing her.

"It's okay," she mutters into the awkward air, her voice being that of a mouse as she diverts her green eyes to the tiled floor.

Jimin steps forward to join the circle that the three were standing in. "We can help you catch this person, I just want to get this over with."

It was surprising to see the two show up here, all the way in Ilsan-ri. But she was grateful for their kind attempt. They just wanted to help and make her feel better, she couldn't get mad at that.

"Thanks, you two," she offers them a sweet smile, "I'm glad you guys are here, you can come eat with me and the other boys of iKON, you haven't got to officially meet them yet!" She just seemed to realize that they hadn't indeed met the other members. Other than Jinhwan eating with them that time, and the fact Jungkook woke up in their dorm, they never officially were introduced, not to every member of iKON.

Jungkook seemed to be thinking about something rather intently, so Jimin cheerily hums for the both of them, "that sounds good, Mi!"

The bright expression on her face was genuine as she jumped around a bit from the excitement she was feeling. She just knew Jimin would love the others, and so would Jungkook if he was in a good mood. He obviously hadn't been when he woke up in pain at their dorm, but it would be different this time.

She always loved the idea of bringing her two close friend groups together. Now she was finally getting the chance, even though there were only two out of seven in one of them. This could be the opening for something great, either way, allowing for her to introduce the other five later on.

So, even though her poor Jinhwan was still up in that hospital room, she found a way to find joy in that horrible day. Even though the psycho was still on the loose, even though she had so many worries, even though her career could be in danger soon — she felt content with her closest friends at her side.

With that in mind, she links an arm in Junhoe's and the other in Jimin's, "let's go!"

And that they did, with Jungkook trailing behind them.

Even though they had bought the largest suite the hotel had to offer, you could only get such a big room in such a small town. It was why the nine adults were rather crowded in the space that the living room was, but they were happy as they ate their take out either way.

Her stomach had been crying for a meal like she just had, and the fact it was her favorite food only made it all that much better.

"Nobody says anything about you, ahjussi."

Many of them start cracking up at the bewildered and annoyed expression that takes over Yunhyeong's face. The bickering of the group never ended, and Soomi wanted to slam her head into the floor from the fact it had begun. 

"Yah, I'm literally the second oldest, why does nobody call Jinhwan ahjussi?!"

"Because he doesn't act like a fucking grandpa," Chan retorts in that sassy tone of his, "he's also not with us right now, making you the eldest, ahjussi."

His taunting, playful words made Yunhyeong frown.

Meanwhile, the Bangtan boys had only listened to what was going on, having a few small conversations here and there. Soomi was still leaning on Jungkook, who was eating his chicken while humming a song she didn't recognize. A part of her wanted to ask him about the song he refused to show her earlier, as it would be something that would get her mind off everything happening other than having to listen to her friends bickering. Those boys never had a filter even when they were around new people, she could only mentally sigh.

She shrugs, not caring much to talk about it since the answer was probably already obvious, "pretty much."

The dark haired prince's chin nearly falls on the floor from how he gawks, "what?! Now I'm an elder?!"

At this point, the boys of iKON were in extreme fits of giggles. Hanbin had stopped eating to bury his face in his hands, wanting to disappear because of how embarrassing these two idiots were. Junhoe was just sitting there as it all went down, probably looking for a place to cut in with his own jokes like he always did. Bobby was laughing so hard that he kept clapping out of disbelief, even laying back on the ground as the hysterics leave his lips, with Donghyuk being a giggly mess right beside him.

Jimin chuckles as he continues to watch the exchange before him, "but they're funny."

He seemed to know it, as he rose a brow inquisitively, "just good, huh?"

She almost physically winced from that sudden deep tone he was using just to bother her. It was clear this was his intention, when he ran his tongue against his bottom lip, and she had to look away so it couldn't affect her anymore.

He really couldn't stop with the games for once second, could he?
