He knew what she really wanted to say, though.





51:00 | first meetings

2013 | the trainee days


Beads of sweat form all over her body, her muscles ache, her breathing heavy. With a groan of pure exhaustion, the young girl's back hits the wall that was lined in mirrors with a clunk, sliding against it until her bottom hit the floor. Unable to stop her abnormal breathing pattern, she uses the back of her hand to wipe sweat that was dripping in streams down her face. Holding her hand in front of her face, she cringes at the sight of her makeup now on her hand instead of her face from the action. 

Oh well, it wasn't like it mattered anyway. As far as she knew, she was the only one still at the company so late. She'd been staying every night, so much her boss - or should she call him CEO-nim? - was starting to worry about her. "I admire your hard work to debut, but let yourself rest," he'd tell her, but she would only shake it off with a reassuring smile.

"Thanks for worrying about me, but I'll be okay, I promise," she would tell him with confidence. He would only chuckle at her hard-working attitude, before patting her on the back. 

They had the same conversation every night for a while, but eventually her boss came to realize she wasn't going to stop staying at the company so late. He told her it was okay and stopped bothering, just that she needed to make sure she turned all the lights off and locked the doors when she left after making sure nobody else was in the building.

So far, she had never seen another soul in the company as late as her. There were a few other trainees here, but they didn't work anywhere near as hard as her. Maybe it was just because she was the newest addition to the company's line of trainees, and the others had been here for so much longer, that she just had a newcomer's spirit to work hard and it would ware off. But she had no intention of ever stopping her late night working, not until she debuted and made herself known.

Even then, sometimes your body gave up. It was exactly what her's did as her muscles were throbbing in every part, and she whines out in pain, leaning her head back against the mirror and still struggling to catch her breathe.

It'll get better in time, she reminds herself. This was only the beginning of her training stages after all, of course she didn't have good endurance and stamina yet. Over time, however, it would build up, so much that one day this would be a piece of cake to her.

Assuring herself of this is what got her to push through the pain she was in. Shifting in her seating position against the wall, she pulls out her phone to check the time. A text from her aunt shows up on her screen, and she purses her lips as she reads over it.

When are you coming home? You've been working so late every night, are they working you that hard?

She sighs as she reads it. It really wasn't her want to lie to anyone, but she didn't have a choice. Until she had a place of her own, she had to tell her aunt she had an actual paying job. If she were to tell the truth of her being a trainee at some small company, she'd get kicked to the curb immediately, or her aunt might do worse - tell her family. The last thing she wanted was go back to New York.

With this all in mind, she types a reply before hitting send.

I'll be home in a few hours maybe, I am just working overtime so I can get out of your hair faster, auntie:)

Turning off her phone, she sets it beside her nearly empty water bottle. Using all of the strength she had regained during her short break, she'd rose to her feet again. 

"Alright," she mutters to herself, peering at her own slim figure in the mirror, "I should do it a few more times just to make sure I have it right."

A breathe of courage leaves her mouth as she spins on one foot, heading over to the stereo. She'd been working on the dance project for her next assessment with the CEO, and she wanted to make sure it was perfect. If you showed continuous progress and impressed him, after all, you'd get that much closer to debuting. Such a thing was exactly her goal, it meant she had to strive to reach it with every waking second she had.

Pressing the play button, the EDM track begins to play again. Looking back to herself in the large mirrors that surrounded her in the tiny dance room, she made sure her facial expression was right before beginning. 

Really, she was never a dancer. Something like dancing always seemed fun to her, but she didn't think she was good at it. 

That didn't mean she couldn't learn, and the only way to do such a thing was practice. Even if it didn't make perfect, it just needed to make her good enough.

Meanwhile, a certain young trainee himself was making his way through the halls of Big Hit Entertainment. He was tired from a long day of practice, having had stayed over night to make sure he really had the group dance down. Even though he was a solid dancer, he still didn't feel like he was up to par with everyone else. Although in reality, he was the top dancer of his group, he just had a gut feeling that he always needed to practice more and more.

Pushing his dark fringe out of his face, he makes his way through the hall, trying to decide which practice room he was going to use. Assuming they would all be empty since most trainees never practiced this late, he was confused at the sight of a light on in one of the rooms.

Being the curious boy he always was since birth, he walks up to the door. It wasn't see through, so he puts his ear to the thin door, a wondrous look on his face. He was well acquainted with most of the trainees, even in the few months he'd been here that wasn't actually very long at all. Most people knew him since it was such a small company, and he was already one of everyone's favorites. Whoever it was in there probably knew of him or they were already friends. After all, he'd been scouted by SM, JYP, and plenty of other companies. It was astonishing to other people when he told them this, and they'd always ask why would you choose such a small company then?

But something about the small company that scouted him as well had been special to his heart. It seemed like a place where you could find a family, a place that he always wanted to be a part of. The big companies were never like that.

Figuring he had to know whoever it was and wouldn't mind some company during his late night practice, he shrugs casually before grabbing the door handle and twisting it. Pushing the door open with his body, the booming EDM music at max volume blasted through his ears as he enters the room.

Whoever it was didn't notice him since the entrance was on the opposite side, away from all the mirrors. Opening his mouth, he's about to yell out when he recognized who it was, but he didn't. 

The thing was, he didn't recognize them.

One thing he had noticed upon coming to Big Hit, was there were no female trainees. He had maybe only seen a few since he had been here, but not recently. Unsure of the reason, he figured the CEO must not be interested in making a girl group, so he just didn't scout females.

This is why he was so surprised to see just that - a girl. Her dark hair went straight to the middle of her back, and she was wearing some of the most casual, baggy clothes he had ever seen on a girl, complete with her white sneakers.



In literally all his years of life, never had he been so abruptly caught off guard by the sight of a girl. Most of them always tried so hard, even when they were doing simple things like going to the store or well, practicing, and he was bewildered to see one look so casual. Like he'd stated previously, though, he seemed to know every trainee - but he'd never seen her in his life until now.

Something inside of him is urging his mouth to move, for him to speak up and say something, but he felt like he was frozen. Time seemed to stop, and he just stood there, watching her dance to the upbeat EDM song that blasted at full volume from the stereo. She had to be new, so why was she so good? Even he didn't improve that fast, after all, he still felt like he wasn't good enough to even think about debuting yet. So how was this girl already looking like that of an idol?

Complete, utter bewilderment still wouldn't be descriptive enough to describe his current emotion. The look on his face was that as if he'd just seen a groundbreaking discovery right before him, she was just too good. He knew why CEO-nim had chosen this girl even if he didn't want to debut a girl group.

The girl finishes the dance, dramatically posing at the end. If someone showed him a video of her and told him she was an upcoming soloist, he would believe them. It was exactly what she looked like, so much that he was left gawking at her like a weirdo as the song ends, and she walked over to turn off the stereo.

Silence falls over the practice room, and the girl is out of breathe as she falls to sit on the floor again. Before she noticed him, he tries to act like he had just walked in the room, his sneakers clicking against the floor as he walks towards her.

The sudden noise in the peaceful air caused her head to jolt up, eyes full of wonder as they land on the boy approaching her. He thought she would say something, maybe like asking him who he was or why he was there, but she didn't even open her mouth. Hair stuck to her face from how much she was sweating, and he could see the messed up makeup smearing on her skin, but yet it didn't make him think any different of her appearance. There was something about this unknown new trainee.

She'd sat there, lost in her own world, staring at him. It was like he'd looked at her when she was dancing.

Stopping a few feet away from her sitting body, he clears his throat, bowing after a moment and introducing himself, "hi, sorry for walking in on you, I just saw someone else was here late and wanted to ask if you wanted some company."

Even after he says this and moments pass, she says nothing. The brunette was just sitting there in her spot on the floor, holding her water bottle that was now empty, and gawking at him intently. Her eyes were narrowed in concentration, and he began to feel self conscious for the first time in his life from how she seemed to be inspecting all of his features.

Not knowing what to do because he was feeling rather awkward, he's about to ask if she was okay because well, she was quiet even though he spoke to her, when the girl hums, "have I seen you somewhere?"

So she does know me.

"Maybe, the CEO likes to brag about me a lot."

A wave of realization washes over her face, "oh," she gasps in remembrance, "yeah, you got scouted by a bunch of big companies, right?"

He only nods, and she makes a sound of disbelief. "That's pretty cool, this one was the only one I could get into."

Thinking it was okay, he gradually falls against the wall to sit beside her, still keeping his space though. "Which one's did you audition for?"

She didn't have to think to reply, "JYP and SM."

"Oh, they tried to scout me, but I declined for a reason," he tries to make her feel better even though her face didn't actually show any sign of distress, "the big companies aren't as - homey - I guess."

The girl doesn't say anything for a while, she was in deep thought about something he didn't know.

After a few minutes, she speaks again, "you didn't have to bow to me, you know."

"Huh?" he blinks at her in confusion, she seems a bit odd. But it wasn't a bad thing to him, this new trainee was sort of cool.

A chuckle leaves her lips as she explains what she meant further, "you bowed, but I'm probably younger than you, so you don't have to - right?" She had started speaking so confidently, but with each word her voice got higher pitched, and she got to the point where she was clearly questioning herself.

Something about her demeanor had been different since she first talked, and he seemed to finally put his finger on it. "You're not from here, are you?"

Finally, she made a different facial expression from having been blank for the last five minutes. "Aw, is it that obvious?" she pouts a bit, looking like a lost puppy, and he had to look away to hide the smile that spread over his face.

"Maybe."

"New York," she says hesitantly after a few seconds, "I'm from New York, I just got here when I got the email that I was accepted here."

He nods in understanding, this girl was obviously Korean but she grew up in America. It explained a lot to him, actually. "I figured you were new, how long have you been here?"

Not looking at him, she fiddles with her fingers that lay in her lap as she mutters, "only a few weeks, sorry if you saw my dancing, I know it's not that great yet," he opens his mouth to begin to assure her it was really great, but she added before he could do so, "what about you, mister sm and jyp?"

Giggling from the name, he shakes his head as he responds, "uh, I think maybe a few months."

She makes an exaggerative sound with her lips, sounding like a pop as she sighs, "wow, I would've thought longer."

Raising a brow, he didn't wait to question, "why's that?"

For the first time since he walked in there, she looked to him again. Meeting his eyes, he noticed that she didn't have the typical brown Korean eyes, her irises were bright green. It was much similar to the color of freshly blooming grass in the spring, a vibrant color he figured had to be contacts.

You can imagine how shocked he was when he found out they weren't.

"I don't know," she's mumbling, studying him again, "something about you gives off a professional vibe."

He wanted to thank her, because he guessed that was a compliment, but he reminded himself of the conversation they had been previously having. "So how old are you, since you said you're probably younger than me?" it might seem sort of weird to ask from her perspective, but he was just asking out of curiosity - nothing more.

The girl didn't seem bothered by it, though. "Eighteen."

She was young.

"Only by a year," he tells her, the news causing her to look him up and down again.

"Weird," she mutters, "you look pretty old."

Should he be offended? "Wah, is that a compliment or not?"

A small giggle leaves her lips as she shrugs, "figure it out."

Shaking his head, he subconsciously seemed to have scooted closer to her, because when he moves to face her so he could ask something important, his hand grazes hers, that had been resting on the side of her body. She seemed to jump a bit at the sudden contact, awkwardly bringing her hand into her lap as she looked away to the opposite side of where he was.

Cursing at himself mentally, he tried to act like it didn't happen as he clears his throat, "so, what's your name, new trainee?"

"Creepy that you want to know, mister sm and jyp."

"Yah, chill with the name, it makes me sound like an ignorant brat," he whines, and she laughs at how he sounded like that of a child. Really, they were children.

Silence for another few seconds, when she informs, "Soomi, and you - or should I just stick with mister sm and jyp?"

Groaning at the name again, he shakes his head as he meets her bright eyes, they really were unique.

He couldn't help it that he was smiling at her like a love struck idiot.

"Jungkook."







52:00 | confidential visit



There seriously was nowhere near enough room for 14 people to stay, even in the biggest suite the hotel had to offer. Thankfully, the guys realized this as they were preparing to head to sleep, so Namjoon had gone down to the lobby and bought the other hotel suite located across the hall. They had no idea what they would've done if it wasn't available, but much to her luck, they scored.

It was logical that the boys of BTS would be staying in the other one while the iKON boys stayed in the current one. The only thing was, Soomi didn't know where she was gonna stay. All of her stuff was still in the iKON's suite since she hadn't moved it since she got here. That being said, it would be easier for her to stay there.

But remembering how badly her old friends so called missed her, and how they still hadn't hung out much even though they spent the entire last few hours with her and iKON, she still felt like it wasn't enough. She saw the boys daily now because she lived with them, but her poor old friends and her only got together on rare occasions.

Although it was risky for her to go stay with them because she had a bad feeling of what would happen, she couldn't resist the urge. Soomi missed her old friends, too.

So after informing her newest friend group of her whereabouts, she made her way across the hallway that night. She was beyond tired, and the boys probably weren't even awake at that point since it was getting so late and everyone had plans tomorrow. They'd taken off from any schedule they had for the next couple of days to come stay with her, so she and everyone were going to go out tomorrow in hopes to get her mind off Jinhwan. Meanwhile, the boys of iKON would stay back at the hospital and watch over in case he woke up.

Soomi hadn't come up with this idea. She wanted to stay and watch over him, too, but all of the thirteen had agreed that it was for the best. The poor girl had too much on her shoulders and they wanted to relieve her of some of that stress.

Upon arriving at the front door, she didn't actually have a plan on what she'd do about Jungkook. There wasn't anyway to avoid him even if she wanted to. It was hard enough to resist him as he was, but adding the way he would always purposely bother her and that stupid hair of his now, how was she supposed to maintain her courage?

It didn't seem right to give into him. Even though her and Jinhwan weren't together and never had been, it still felt like it. A part of her still felt off without him, but yet she didn't feel right without Jungkook either. The endless, difficult decision only continued to weigh down her mental state as she sighed. Still, it wouldn't be okay for her to be with Jungkook right now.

Right?

Heaving out a sigh, the world seemed to be mad at her as she had looked up to the sound of the door opening. Assuming it would be Jimin, she was ready to tell him about everything that was bothering her right now. Her rant would probably have gone on for hours with all that was on her mind, all the way from this horrid psycho to the decision she just couldn't seem to make.

"Soomi, you decided to stay here," there's a giddy, child like smile on Jungkook's face from the sight of her. Her stomach drops when she meets those eyes of his. Just like she thought, you could never get away from Jeon Jungkook.

She only responds with a nod, a close lipped grin on her face as she enters. Jungkook had stepped to the side of the door so he could allow her in. Her eyes rake across the suite, which was pretty much the same as the iKON one with just a few tiny differences like furniture. The modernized decorated hotel suite was nearly pitch dark except for a singular lamp that was on in the living room, providing them light to see each other in the dim air. 

Her back was to her ex fiance as she walks deeper into the large living room, not knowing where exactly she was even going to sleep so she just set her bag beside one of the sofa's. Assuming it was the same as the other, there were two rooms, one with two queen sized bed and then one with a singular king sized bed. Knowing her old friends well, she had a feeling they had decided who slept where by playing rock paper scissors, they'd decided everything that way since their trainee days, after all.

From the fact she'd been silent, Jungkook frowns a bit. He knew there was probably a lot on her mind. Jimin had spoken to him before he went to sleep when the boys came to their own room, and the words of Soomi's best friend repeated in his head as he turns to stare at the back of her head.

She's going through a lot, Jungkook, let her breathe and stop making it harder on her.

His competitive, possessive traits were just going to have to calm themselves. It would be hard for him to just turn them off, but if it was really troubling her so much, he would do it.

"How are you feeling?" he asks, walking closer to her even though she still wasn't facing him. Just because he would stop messing with her, didn't mean he was going to stop showing her affection altogether. Everyone knew he couldn't do that even if he wanted to. "I am," she finally breathes out, an evident flirtatious vibe in her voice, "I would love if you did."

The woman was beyond confused at his words. There's a slight fear in her eyes as she looks to his phone screen, "excuse me, what are you talking about?"

Jungkook ignores her, instead dialing something on his phone before putting it to his ear.

"Hello, officer, I've found the woman who drugged a man and put him into a coma," he's humming to them on the other line, "yes, regarding the incident yesterday," another few seconds pass as he hears what they're asking him, "yes, at the Hilton, I have recorded proof of her admitting to the crime."

"We'll be there shortly."

"Thank you!" He cheerily calls before ending the call. Only then did Jungkook turn back to the woman, who was petrified with shock and fear. She wasn't looking at him, her eyes were fixated on the ground or something behind him as she seemed to be trembling, in some sort of trance from what she realized what was happening.

"H-how—," She's muttering to herself or maybe Jungkook, "I-I didn't do it — I didn't m-mean to..." her voice trails off as she whines like a lost puppy. However, it was hard for him to have any sympathy for her. Whether she was forced to do it or not, she still gave into it. It was still her fault even partly.

"I don't care for what you have to say, but I'm sure the cops would love to hear it," he tells her whether she was even speaking to him.

Turning on his heel, Jungkook begins to make his way towards the exit doors. As if on queue, the wailing of sirens is heard in the distance, seeming to confirm his previous words.

"W-Wait, please," the woman's voice suddenly calls out, and there's an unimpressed look on his face when he turns to look to her again, "please I — I didn't do it, she forced me!"

He blinks at her a few times, this was what he thought happened, but another idea comes to mind.

Walking towards her, the sirens only get closer as he does so. Not wasting anytime, he rushes out the question, "She? What did she look like?"

This is what Soomi needed to know. This was the key to who was doing this to her and had to him only over a year ago.

She only trembled from the words that left his mouth. Jungkook peers down at her with hopeful eyes, waiting for her to say anything. But she was practically traumatized, frozen like some sort of statue.

Until she mumbles out, "I-I can't tell you — she said she'd kill me..."

"Police!" The sudden yell cuts him off from saying anything else, the doors of the hotel bursting open. Jungkook turns to see the authorities he called all rushing in, "Heo Hyelin, you're under arrest for carrying of illegal drugs and attempted murder!"

Two of the officers rush to the girl they'd just named, grabbing her arms and forcing them behind her back. There's a clicking sound of the handcuffs, and she hadn't even tried to fight their actions as they dragged her out of the hotel.

It was sort of disturbing to witness. She looked like her soul had left her body, like she'd died.

"Thank you for calling us, young man," the offer he spoke to on the phone hums, patting his shoulder, "it was tragic what happened to that man yesterday, I hope he can have a safe recovery knowing who did it to him is behind bars," he's saying, "but please send the recording to us, we'll review it before taking her into questioning back at the station."

Only nodding, the officer had sent him a close lipped smile before turning to walk away.

"Wait, sir," he calls out, "I think there was someone else involved."

The officer blinks at him in curiosity, "you mean someone made her do it?"

Pursing his lips, he nods. "I just thought you should know that. Also, if you find anything, could you call this number," he's mumbling, turning to the counter to take a napkin before using a random pen to scribble Soomi's number on it. Walking to the officer, he holds it out, "it's the number of a close friend of the man in the coma, if the woman admits to who made her do it, she would be glad to know."

Humming in understanding, he takes the napkin from the boy's hand. "I'll make sure to let her know."

Letting out a breathe of gratitude, he sends him a grateful smile, "thank you."

Watching the police men leave, he was left to stand in the rather dead hotel coffee shop by himself. A yawn leaves his lips from the lack of sleep he received last night, but for once, Jungkook felt victorious. He felt like he'd done something good, like he was one step closer to finding whoever this monster was.

With that, he makes his way out of the hotel, ready to actually get some exercise by running back to the one they were all staying at. He hoped Soomi would be glad to hear the good news.

It was all for her, after all.

"Well, what do you think?" Yoongi hums, his eyes wandering to Soomi as his hands leave the keyboard of the laptop. Soomi's eyes become glassy as she stares at the boy before her. As if their talks last night weren't enough, he'd done this for her and Jinhwan. It wasn't something she would expect from Jungkook, and it had her nearly bursting into tears.

"Jungkook," she could only manage to whisper, "thank you..."

He only flashes her that smile of his, one she was more than ecstatic to see on his face in that moment. Unable to hide her joy, she scoots closer to him again, not caring at all about the fact he was still sweaty from his exercising session. Her small arms find their way around his neck, where she squeezes the life out of him - but he still wasn't affected by her small amount of strength.

His heart on his sleeve, he snuggles his head into her hair as he accepts the hug. Soomi, his mind screams, I'll find whoever's caused all of this, I promise.

That he would, Jungkook was only one step closer. He was going to make this person pay, for hurting her, hurting him, and ruining the best thing he'd ever had - an engagement to the girl he loved. 

He'd make sure of that.

The maknae only shrugs, a toothy grin on his lips.

Like usual, the pointless conversation disappears into the air of the living room hotel. 56:00 | finally united



People didn't hesitate to move out of the way from the sight of a wild brunette rushing down the hallway. Her bag flies every which way on her shoulder, hitting people with a whack as she zooms past them. In her opinion, she should've been here already, even though everyone agreed she was going to spend a 'relaxation' day with her old friends. The entire relaxation part had already been demolished anyway from the fact Jungkook got the barista woman sent to the police station.

When New Years struck, the boys of Bangtan and iKON had all gotten together at their massive mansion located in the country side of Seoul. It had a great view of the Han river, and they popped fireworks as they drank and had a great time. Soomi even drank a few drinks, not enough to get drunk since her tolerance was so high, but enough to find herself letting go. For the first time, that night, she had forgotten about everything.

Unfortunately for everyone, the day after, they'd been called to their respective companies for the KCON meeting. It was no surprise that they all were attending whether they liked it or not. With how big they were all growing with Korean music in general, it would be insane for them to pass up the opportunity.

All the while, Soomi hadn't heard one word from her secret stalker.

So it brought her here, January 4, as she walks through the airport. Her head aches from the thoughts wandering through her mind, but she forces herself to have a bright smile on since there were so many fans gathered to say goodbye at the airport.

Having already sent off her luggage, she was left carrying her take on bag and her phone, while trying to gather the gifts fans tried to give to her. Sometimes they didn't get to, though, since she had so many body guards surrounding her and pushing off anyone who got with in feet of her.

"I love you, Soomi!"

"Have a safe flight, queen!"

They all scream out messages, taking pictures when they get a good angle. She waves and yells out thank you's, trying to smile nicely for each of their photos. It was something she was used to.

Finally, they walk through the gates to head onto the plane. This meant no fans were back there, and she sighs out as she could finally breath normally and stop smiling.

Pulling her phone out of her back pocket, she rushes onto the messaging app.

N E W    Y O R K





"What the fuck do you want?!" the girl curses out in a whisper, her green eyes bulging out of their sockets as she rushes forward onto the porch, shutting the front door behind her. In a panic, she places both her hands on their chest, pushing the figure back until they were out of sight of any of the front windows of the house. Once they're in a place where they can't easily be seen, she holds a hand to her head in distress, "I told you to stop coming here, Solar isn't coming back, it's been five fucking years!"

No sign of emotion shows on the person's face before her. No, the boy only raises a brow, not caring much for what just came out of her mouth.

"No shit," he deadpans, "that's not what I'm here for, Chaerin."

A sigh leaves her lips, and she crosses her arms over her chest impatiently. "Then what do you want, Sunwoo? I told you I didn't have any interest in speaking to you," her harsh tone grows softer with each word, until it was a mumble, "all you do is remind me of her," she finishes dully, her eyes diverting to her feet.

Either way, everything around her reminded her of Soomi. You simply couldn't get away from it, she was always there somehow. The eldest daughter of the family had left a permanent scar on not only Chaerin's heart, but everyone else's, too.

There's a low chuckle from the tall boy standing before her. Shocked at the fact he had the audacity to laugh at her, she's about to knee him where the sun doesn't shine, when he stops her from doing such by speaking, "and you think you don't remind me of Solar? You've got the same eyes, just a bit lighter," he hums, his eyes wandering all over her face as if he was inspecting her features, "the same lips, too. I almost see her when I look at you."

She only rolls her eyes at him, knowing well she didn't actually look anything like her sister. Chaerin and Soomi had a clear difference. The only things they had that were similar was exactly what Sunwoo just mentioned.

"Yein, though," he shakes his head in disbelief, "she's like a replica."

Now that wasn't a lie.

"I know," Chaerin laments, "there's not a thing they don't have in common."

By this point, the two of them were so deep in thought about the girl that Sunwoo seemed to forget what he came here for. Before he could begin to remember, though, an abrupt marvel is heard from behind them, along with the sound of a car being locked.

"Sunwoo, Chaerin!" Juyeon calls as he walks up the driveway, slapping Sunwoo's back as a greeting and only grinning at his sister, "what the hell are you two doing together?"

The short brunette only shrugs as she motions to Sunwoo, "I don't know, this idiot keeps showing up asking about Solar like she's gonna randomly show up one day."

His previously bright face deflates in a second from the name that rolls of her lips. Juyeon clears his throat, uncomfortable thinking about his sister as he sighs, "o-oh, well, it's been five years dude," his voice shakes a bit when he informs Sunwoo of this obviously known fact, "and she still hasn't shown up, so I think you're shit outta luck."

Chaerin watches as he turns away, practically running up the steps to the mansion and zooming inside. She pursed her lips, feeling bad that she so casually brought up their sister in front of Juyeon. If she felt guilty, there was no telling how he felt, she could only imagine. After all, it had all been his idea. 

Juyeon and Soomi had never really been close. He didn't think of what kind of consequences his accusations could have back then, and it only back fired in his face, in all of their faces.

And they could never take it back. Knowing what he felt like made her want to go comfort her poor brother, she didn't want him to do anything dumb, after all. The siblings had deemed to take care of each other after the disappearance of their big sister, no matter what.

"Chae-"

"Look, Sunwoo, I don't have time to talk about Solar with you," she sighs as she turns back to him from having watched Juyeon disappear inside, "I need to go check on him."

Not fully grasping what was going on, he wondered why exactly Juyeon got like that from the mention of his sister. He understood they missed her, sure, it was awful what happened. But it had always been weird to him how the only one who left was Solar, not any of the others. He knew they had all been involved, after all.

He got that he missed her, but was it really still so bad that he'd immediately cry upon hearing her name?

Or was there more to the story he had yet to hear?

When he doesn't say anything, the girl before him heaves out a deep breath, before spinning on her heel and heading back up the steps to her house.

"Chaerin, wait!" he calls, but she ignored him as she disappeared inside.

A defeated look on his face, only then did Sunwoo remember what he truly came here for in the first place. Slowly, his eyes wander to the pieces of paper he held in his hands, the pieces that would help him solve the empty spot that'd been left in his heart.

Although he wasn't sure what to do with one extra, since Chaerin and Juyeon clearly weren't going to budge. He figured they probably didn't even have any idea.

They didn't know what he did. Little did Sunwoo know, they had secrets, too.

Pulling out his phone, he stares down at the fragile papers as he walks back to his car. Climbing inside, he finds the familiar contact while tapping his foot against the floor of the car. Without hesitation, he taps call over the name - Jaehyun.











63:00 | so close but yet so far


N E W     Y O R K 


The day of KCON approached scarily fast. Thanks to the fact they probably should've flew over earlier, the friends didn't have any time to get over their jet lag when they landed in the city. It had been right to rehearsals for them, where they all met up with the Bangtan boys. Everyone agreed they hadn't gotten to do anything since they just got there, so they'd go out to eat afterwards and walk around the city.

It was likely they would get spotted in the city, but since it wasn't prohibited for either of them to be around each other, nobody cared at that point. The media seemed to know Soomi was friends with both the groups of guys whether she liked it or not — they just didn't know to what extent when it came to Jungkook and Jinhwan.

"Are you ready for this?" Jungkook had asked her, placing a hand on her shoulder comfortingly. He knew what she was feeling as everyone piles out of the van. She'd rode with her old friends to the restaurant, so they had to meet up with the others.

Stepping into the fresh American air, she inhales deeply, holding it for a long second as if taking it in before exhaling. Her green eyes rake over her surroundings, and Jungkook didn't mind that she hadn't said a word in reply to him. He only watches her as she turns in circles as they all walk towards the restaurant, gawking at all the familiar sights.

"Aw, look at Soo," Yunhyeong is gushing, "her homesickness is cured."

He gains a few looks from the ones who have any idea of how untrue that was. Nobody blamed him since he didn't know the truth. Soomi stops looking around from his words, finding her thoughts wander back to her family.

Did she want to see them? Would she even be able to?

It was something she'd been debating on endlessly since she was invited. She tried talking to Jungkook and Jimin about it, but they both ended up telling her the same thing.

"If you believe you're ready, Mi, it's now or never."

But she couldn't be so sure if she was ready. At the same time, she didn't want to miss an opportunity to see them again. Even though a part of her was still angry and hurt — in the end, they were still her family whether she liked it or not.

Although she had found a new family in the friends she was surrounded by, it was obvious it wasn't the same as her biological one. Nothing could compare to your own parents, your own siblings. She couldn't replace them if she tried.

"Stop stressing, Soomi-ah," the voice of Jinhwan breaks through her head.

Looking up, she hadn't noticed him walking on her left, with Jungkook to her right. The feeling of the two of them both being right beside her sent her stomach into a frenzy, and she tries to distract herself with other things as she sends the caramel boy a smile, "I'm not, I'm okay."

"You better be, hoe!" She's nearly knocked over by Junhoe when he pushes her from behind.

Stumbling a bit forward from how scarily strong he was compared to her tiny self, she catches herself. Annoyance is written clear over her face when she turns to glare at the giant, "you're lucky I'm too hungry to beat you up right now," she points an incriminating finger at him, narrowing her eyes.

Junhoe only raises a brow as he's still in fits of giggles, "oh please, as if you could ever."

"You wanna fucking find out?!"

Nobody bothered to stop the two when Soomi began to chase Junhoe in circles around the parking lot they were walking on. Some of them were laughing at the idiots that they called friends, while others — like poor Hanbin — only covered his face in embarrassment. Sometimes he really wished they didn't do shit like this.

It wasn't like the petite girl could actually hurt him even if she caught him. There was no point in Junhoe running away from her to begin with, but it was all just part of the fun.

"Why the fuck would you call me a hoe when it's literally in your name?!" Soomi is yelling at her best friend as she continues to run after him. He ended up being too fast for her since his legs were 80% of his body.

"Hey, I didn't say I wasn't!" He shoots back, finally quitting his running because he grew tired.

Figuring that was the end of it as Soomi stops to walk beside him, panting as well from the exercise, everyone's eyes widen at the sound of a yelp leaving the talk boys lips. Turning back to the two, the friends burst into fits of hysterics at the sight of her grabbing onto his ear, pinching it as she pulls his head side ways.

"Okay, okay, I'm sorry!" Junhoe is whining like a baby as he tries to get his ear out of her fingers.

Soomi didn't seem to convinced as she pinched it harder with her sharp nails. A curse leaves the boys lips, and she chuckles at the fact she was finally winning against him, "you should be, whore."

With that, she lets go of the pouty Junhoe.

"Talk about rude," he's muttering as they all enter the restaurant after that ridiculous fiasco.

"Soomi-ah, wait!" The honey tone causes her to halt where she had been about to enter the van. 

Slowly, she turns in confusion to meet the eager looking Jinhwan. There's a glint in his eyes, and the night sky was already glaring down upon them since they had gotten here in the middle of the day. By the time rehearsals ended and they went to eat, it was already night in New York City.

But Soomi didn't mind it being dark. It was the prettiest that way. She'd always said the best NYC came out when it's night — for many reasons.

Pursing her lips, she raises a brow at the excited boy, "yes, Jinani?"

He looks to the van instead of responding to her, doing some sort of hand motion. Soomi jumps from the sound of a revving engine behind her, turning in shock when the van drives away.

"That was our ride—," she points in confusion, not understanding why he would do what he just did.

Still, the short boy doesn't inform her of anything as he steps forward. Holding up a hand, a yellow vehicle stops against the curb with in a second.

A triumphant grin takes over his face as he opens the back door, motioning inside as he corrects, "no, this is our ride."

Completely bewildered at whatever he was doing, she honestly didn't care. Climbing inside, she offers a greeting to the taxi driver as Jinhwan climbs in next to her. A yawn leaves her lips, and she leans her head on his shoulder as he mutters some address to the driver.

It wasn't a lie that she was from New York, clearly, but when she said New York she meant the upper east side. The city was a big place, and the only part she really knew like the back of her hand was the part she was from.

But for some reason, she hadn't paid attention to whatever address the boy said to the driver. One, because he made sure to say it so quiet she couldn't make out any words, and second, because she was too tired to make an effort to. Whatever he was planning, she figured it was better off being a surprise anyway.

"Are you tired from the trip?" Jinhwan asks, his hand caressing her thigh as they drive through the busy night streets of New York, noticing she was bound to fall asleep on his shoulder.

Indeed, she was getting rather comfy on his coat. It was so soft that it made a great pillow for her, and she wouldn't mind a good sleep. Soomi hadn't slept on the plane ride like everyone else because of how stressed she was.

But now, her body was catching up with her. No matter how many thoughts filled her mind, it was going to pass out anyway.

"Yeah," she only whispers, closing her green eyes as she waits for dreamland to overcome her. It usually took a long time to get from place to place in NYC anyway, she knew this well. So she probably had time for a nap, right?

Soomi was thankful for the power nap she got. Only around twenty five minutes later, however, was Jinhwan nudging her side gently, trying to wake her up.

"We're here, Soo, wake up."

"Baby, get up," he repeats again when the first attempt didn't work. As if she had been awake the whole time, her eyes shoot open from the word, not believing she really just heard it fall from his lips.

She has to mentally recover, it'd been a while since Jinhwan used any names like that.

Paying the driver, they both offer goodbyes as they climb out of the vehicle. His hand finds a way to hers, and she rubs her eyes from still being half asleep. Blinking a few times to make sure she could see clearly, Soomi takes that time to take in where it was he had taken her.

"So..." she's starting to say, when she realizes where they were. Her mouth falls agape from shock at the sight of the place, and she could only peer up at it like she had seen something astonishing.

The boy beside her watches her expression with a giddy smile.

"Jinhwan," she gasps, "I can't believe you remembered me mentioning this place."

The few times she had ever told him anything about her family was when she talked about the good memories she had. A good amount of those memories took place in this exact ice cream parlor that they were standing in front of, a place she didn't think she would ever come back to. Soomi and her siblings used to sit inside of it after school, laughing and making jokes or talking about drama and other things. The parlor had been their safe place from their parents when they were kids.

"Come on, let's go inside," Jinhwan tugs at her hand, snapping her out of her gawking state.

She didn't hesitate to walk with him towards the door. He holds it open for her, and the two enter as if they were children.

Walking right up to the counter, she already knew what she wanted. "I want two scoops of strawberry and one cheesecake with gummy bear toppings, please," she recites, and if the cashier didn't look up they would've thought she was a kid. Her voice was so tiny that it made you want to squeeze her, it was exactly what Jinhwan did as he wraps an arm around her.

Putting in the order, the cashier looks to him. Not knowing much about the place, he only hums, "I'll just have the same."

Soomi bounces up and down on her feet as she watches them put together the order. She and her siblings used to always all order the same thing, and they would all combine their ice creams to make the ultimate ice cream castle. Just thinking of how stupid they were brought a goofy smile on her face.

Before she knew it, the worker slides the two cups of ice cream scoops over the counter after Jinhwan paid yet again. Soomi would usually bother him about letting her pay instead, but she was far too distracted to even remember you had to pay.

"Let's sit over here," she urges, dragging him over to a familiar booth.

Sliding into the booth together, the brunette excitedly starts digging into her ice cream. She was inhaling it like it was the first thing she was eating in years, even though they literally just came from a restaurant.

He giggles at her cute mannerisms, shaking his head as he picks up his own spoon. Sticking a spoonful of the ice cream in his mouth, it ended up tasting better than he expected.

"Good right?" Soomi notices the look on his face, and he only nods in confirmation. Still eating her own, she admits gratefully, "I'm glad you took me here, Jinan, thank you."

Meeting her bright eyes, he shrugs, "sure, I wanted to help make this trip better for you since you've been stressing so much."

Her heart melts from his words. She could almost cry in that moment as she could only peer up at the angelic soul that Jinhwan was.

"I know there's a lot going on, and I can't help or don't even know everything but," he takes another bite, "that doesn't mean I'm not here. I always notice when you're down, and it breaks my heart when there's nothing I can do to help," he admits dully before piping up again, "so I just want to help you move forward, I know you tend to overthink the worst. But I'm here to make sure you don't weigh yourself down so much, I care about you, silly," she was confused as to why he was calling her silly.

Suddenly, she feels his thumb against her chin. Jinhwan wipes off a piece of ice cream with a chuckle, before finishing, "I hope coming here gives you the strength to fight what you're going through, Soomi, and if it doesn't, I hope my love for you can instead."

If she wasn't gone then, she was nowhere to be seen now. Soomi was a puddle of goo on the ground as she scoots to the side, enclosing the space between her and Jinhwan.

She squeezes him like her life depended on it, and right then, she never wanted to let go.

"Thank you," she mumbles, "thank you, thank you, thank you."

It was as if those were the only words she knew. What more could she say to him? She was at a complete loss.

"Stop thanking me," he's giggling, knowing well she had no idea what to say, "just eat your ice cream, dummy."

Pulling out of the hug, his arm remains around her as she picks her spoon back up. It didn't take her longer than a minute to eat the rest of it.

"There," she says victoriously, "ugh, it's as good as I remember."

The two lovers stay in the ice cream parlor for another good while. Even though they finished their treat, they were just having fun talking and enjoying each other's presence. Soomi was able to let go of her worries even if it was only for a second, and she had him to thank for that.

"Ready to go, or do you want to stay a bit longer?" Jinhwan asks, already rising to his feet so he could go throw away the trash, "we can always come back," he assures her.

The girl rises to her feet, looking around one last time at the parlor.

"We can go, but we definitely have to come back before we leave NYC."

"That's fine by me," he glistens, grabbing her hand again as they head towards the exit and he chunks their empty ice cream cups in the trash can.

Just as the two leave, they pass a familiar two figures. Soomi had been nuzzling her head into Jinhwan's chest as he had his arm wrapped around her since the weather was so cold, trying to steal all of his warmth.

The moon peers down upon the world, particularly New York. A sigh fills the sole air as the little girl walks, her hand in her older brothers as they make their way towards the entrance of the ice cream parlor.

She felt weird, although she didn't know what it was. Juyeon wasn't paying attention, too focused on something on his phone to see how Yein was turning every which way.

Her green eyes suddenly fixated on two people, it looked like a couple. Squinting, the young girl tries to take in any of their features, but it was impossible since their backs where to her.

For some reason, she couldn't stop staring at them.

She should've noticed. She should've noticed the long, flowing brown hair that was all too familiar to her. She should've noticed the familiar sashay, the familiar bag that hung from her shoulders.

She should've noticed it was her big sister.


64:00 | composing the plan


"Welcome everyone, to KCON New York 2019!" the arena erupts into screeches of the fans, high pitched thunders of their voices in unison echoing across the massive building as the robot announcer goes on from the intercoms, "please welcome your hosts, Joshua and Vernon!"

Soomi watches as the two english speaking members of Seventeen make their way onto the stage. The second they step an inch into public view, more screams explode from the audience. She was honestly worried about getting a migraine having to listen to it, was Korean music seriously this big now? Last time she was here, they didn't need an arena half this big, now it was too full, with even people sitting outside.

Someone like her didn't get stage fright. She'd never felt a day of worry in her life only until this psycho came into it. Just the thought of what could happen, what would happen, had her on edge. It was bad enough there were so many people she had to perform in front of, in her home town, which actually made her a bit conscious. Now, she was adding the fact this person - whoever they may be - was going to expose her life to the world.

How would she get through this? To think she had no idea what exactly they found out. Soomi tries to remind herself of the talks she'd had with Jimin, Jungkook, and Jinhwan. They had all said the same general thing; that whoever this was probably didn't have access to whatever she thought they did. Although this could be true, she didn't know how powerful this person was, what if they really did dig it up?

Her past, the one she so desperately tried to get away from, was it catching up with her after all?

"Mi, hey," she jumps at the sudden contact of a hand on the small of her back. Not realizing she was being dragged somewhere until he was forcing her to sit, "here, drink this, you look pale."

Blinking a few times, she slowly reaches out to take the water bottle. Twisting off the cap, Soomi only mumbles a thanks before practically chugging half of it down. Exhaling deeply in satisfaction, the girl twists the cap on again, setting it aside before looking to Jungkook, who took the seat beside her, "where did you even come from?" she quizzes blankly. She'd been watching the frantic movement of everyone and what was going on on-stage by herself for the last hour, so much she hadn't seen any of the guys around.

"I was in the dressing room getting makeup done," he explains, "that's where the others are right now, too, and probably your other friends."

She only nods, pursing her lips as she rakes her eyes over their surroundings. To think, the last time she was here-

"-Soomi," Jungkook rips her head out of her thoughts when he speaks up abruptly. Her eyes are curious when she looks to him, wondering what was with that certain glint in his tone of voice. The maknae is holding up his hand, and she was confused on why until she saw his ring finger.

Holding a hand over her mouth, she hurriedly pushes his hand back down into his lap with the other. About to have had a heart attack right then and there, she's exasperated, "why are you wearing that - are you crazy?!"

Giggles are all she receives from the taunting boy. She wished then that his doe eyes weren't so twinkly, as maybe then she could actually stay mad at him for more than a second. Those brown irises of him, brightening more under the lights above them, and he diverts them down to his lap, where he looks at the ring on his finger. 

"Something told me to wear it today," he shares fervently, "it brings me back to better times."

It had been just what her mind was on. He wasn't wrong at all; the last time they were here was when they got engaged, but it was also the time when she kissed her best friend. Although it had been so confusing for her back then, there was no denying how happy she was, even though the pressure of seeing her family again had still weighed her down. At least then, she didn't have this many more worries on her shoulders. Now, she was running out of strength to the point she felt as if she could barely walk anymore.

"That's cute," is all she says for a second, staring at her feet because she knew she wouldn't be able to meet his gaze, "just - don't let anyone see it, you know we denied the engagement accusations."

"I won't, Mi, don't worry about it," he assures her calmly, "we have bigger things to focus on, like finding whoever this is that's trying to mess with you tonight."

Upon the mention, she heaves out a long sigh. It was true, if they wanted to stop this, there was only one way to do it. 

"How would we ever?" she frowns, muttering in a complete loss of hope, "it's not like we can get back to the produ-"

"-Soomi, you're a fucking genius."

A bewildered look slaps onto her face. 

"Are you insane?" she asks, holding a hand up to rest it on his forehead as if he was sick, "they aren't going to let you in there."

But there was an intense look in his eyes that let her know he did not care about anything she just said. Jungkook is in extreme focus, creasing his brows as he thinks hard. "Well, I wouldn't think that whoever this person is has free access there, either," his statement makes Soomi's mouth form into an o shape. He's right, she realizes, not unless their stalker was some sort of KCON producer themselves.

Which was very unlikely.

Still, she didn't understand his thoughts. "Okay, but what are you planning to do?" she cautiously questions him, growing worrisome of the devious look taking over his expression.

Not saying a word to her, Jungkook gloriously jumps to his feet. The look on his face seemed to show he thought he came up with the most genius thing ever thought of, as he turns to face the girl still remaining on the bench. 

"I'm gonna fix this, okay?" he leans down to meet her eyes, and Soomi opens her mouth to ask him yet again what exactly he was planning. But she didn't get a chance to, when Jungkook only caresses her cheek before spinning on his heel and practically bolting towards the dressing room hall.

Her hand reaches up to rub the spot he'd just touched, and she could only sigh at where he'd just ran off to, probably to get some of the others involved in his antics, "please don't do anything stupid, Kookie."

Meanwhile, the youngest boy of Bangtan's shoes click against the concrete flooring. His eyes wander from room door to room door, reading every name carefully as he searches for the one he needed. Sometimes, he wondered why the hell they didn't just put the names in alphabetical order, it would make this a lot fucking easier.

Slowing to a walk at this point, he checks behind him every so often to make sure no staff was watching whatever he was doing. He didn't need anyone to ask what he was up to or see where he'd be going, it could get him caught and ruin the great plan he'd came up with in only a mere minute.

You know what they said, drastic times call for drastic measures, and Jungkook would call this a rather treacherous one. Whatever it was that this person didn't for sure have on Soomi, but still could have, seemed to be rather serious even though he didn't know the extent. This is why he needed to make sure he ended this. He'd catch whoever this was, once and for all, and everything would be back to normal.

Finally finding the door after having felt like he was walking for miles, a breath of relief leaves his lips. Knocking a few times, when he gets so response, he realized he didn't have the time to wait anyway. Twisting the handle, Jungkook carelessly marches in, having full awareness of the name on the door; iKON.

"Oh, that's probably our manager-nim now - Jungkook?!" Donghyuk had been saying, as it sounded like they were missing their manager or something. The second his eyes fall on the boy standing at the doorway, blatant confusion overcomes his expression.

The others look up from having heard the name, thinking their friend was crazy. At the sight of the exact boy he'd just mentioned, they end up all gawking, too.

"Hi, Jungkook, what's up?" Hanbin is the first to break the silence of everyone staring at him like he was some sort of ghost.

"You haven't seen our manager by chance, have you?" Yunhyeong raises a brow, a hopeful look on his face, "she's gone MIA on us suddenly."

Not caring much for wherever their stupid manager was, he only shakes his head. The brown eyes of Jeon Jungkook were only looking at one person, a boy that was sitting in the corner of the room on his phone. He was either scrolling or texting someone, probably Soomi asking how she was, and didn't bother to even give him a greeting like the rest of them had.

He couldn't blame him, he probably would've done the same thing.

"Jinhwan," the other six in the room nearly fall over from hearing that was what Jungkook came into their room for. The last thing anyone would think is that he wanted to talk to their eldest, which is why they're even more shocked from his next proposal, "I need your help."

The boy blinks at him, his head gradually rising from his phone. His brows furrow, and he exchanges a glance with Junhoe, who was probably the most confused out of all of them, knowing the full scoop of what went on with the two boys and Soomi (perks of being her best friend.) He was horrified that they were about to go fight each other or something as his hyung as rose to his feet after a second, "uh, alright, what's up?"

Walking over towards Jungkook, if it was any other time, they would laugh at the saddening height difference. But everyone was too worried about the whereabouts of their missing manager and the fact the two boys were associating with each other in the first place. As if the day wasn't already going to be weird enough.

"Follow me, I'll explain to you on the way," Kook had been saying as he makes his way back towards the exit. Jinhwan, still not having any idea what it was he wanted, only hums an agreeing noise before the two exit, closing the door behind them.

Meanwhile, the six that were left only stare at the door. "Does anyone feel fucking lost right now?" Bobby blurts, and the rest of them agree or nod immediately.

Kicking his feet back in the chair, he leans them atop the table in front of where he was sitting. "Probably has something to do with the whole Soomi's stalker thing."

"No shit," Chanwoo looks to Junhoe, who sent him a glare from his sarcasm.

"You know what, pal? I'll step on you right now."

"Dude, that doesn't work on me, we're like the same height."

"Suck my ass."

Hanbin was rubbing his temples from the bickering that had already begun, "can you guys - now is not the time," he pleads, before focusing back on the current situation, "I'm sure they're going to see her or something, but we need to figure out where the hell our manager is so we know what time we're going on stage."

"I'm going to throw your PC off a cliff when we get home," but the arguing wasn't over, even though their leader had begged them to shut up.

"Try it, and you'll never seen your Bob Dylan vinyls again."











65:00 | lost and found



"So, where exactly are we going?" Jinhwan asks blankly, still trailing behind the much taller boy as he walks frantically. They had taken multiple flights of steps, gone down many hallways, and were now heading down an endless path that he had absolutely no idea headed to. It didn't help that he had yet to really tell him anything, only saying it's for Soomi, over and over like he was stuck in some sort of hypnosis.

Sneakers clicking against the concrete of whatever floor they were on by this point, Jungkook exhales with determination as he explains, "to the developer room."

The caramel haired boy is even more lost.

"What?"

Jungkook looks back at him, a taint of annoyance on his face. "You know, where they cast stuff on the screens at and speak into the intercom," he says almost mockingly, as if Jinhwan should know this since he was apparently so much older and wiser.

Not pleased with his tone, he narrows his eyes, trying not to let the devious boy get to him because he was well aware of his games. "No fucking shit, I'm asking what your reasoning is for going there," he snaps.

His hard tone didn't bother Jungkook in the slightest. 

"Well, I figured that's where whoever has been stalking Soomi will be at," he informs his thought process to him, and he only peers at him intently as they walk side by side down the everlasting hallway, "you know, since they said they were going to expose her, it's not like they're gonna be going on stage themselves and doing it. That means there's only one place they could be."

By this point, he fully gathered the extent of Jungkook's plan. Jinhwan was impressed he came up with something like that.

"That's pretty smart for someone like you to think of."

Jungkook halts in his tracks, raising a brow tauntingly as he spins to face the shorter boy. "Huh, someone like me?" he repeats his words in a question, as if wanting him to say them again while meeting his eyes.

But despite their height difference, Jinhwan remained unbothered by his attempt to intimidate him. "Uhuh," he shrugs as if it wasn't a big deal and he wasn't insulting his competition, "I've just heard you're not the brightest around."

The younger one rolls his eyes, turning around to start walking again since his attempt hadn't worked. Knowing him though, he always had many tricks, particularly remarks, up his sleeve. Running his tongue across his bottom lip, there's a smirk on his lips when he hums, "at least I know I make Soomi feel the best."

He didn't need to turn around to know that ticked Jinhwan off. Neither of them were oblivious to the fact she had slept with both of them multiple times. It wasn't something they could get mad at her about, since she had feelings for both of them and usually, it was them tempting her. If anything, it just made them mad at each other, not Mi.

"I wouldn't be so sure of that."

By this time, they reach the developers doors. His hand is reaching for the handle, completely ignoring the sign on the door that read in giant red lettering; do not enter, personnel only.

Even though they had a much more important task on their hands than arguing over something so trivial, he never lost an argument, or his pride.

"Did you not hear her screaming my name that night when you got ba-"

His words aren't cut off from getting hit, surprisingly. They're cut off by Jinhwan when the two of them open the door, being faced with what was on the other side.

It could've gone horribly wrong in many ways. They could've been faced with the actual producers and developers of KCON, who would most likely not be thrilled to be bothered by them. It would've been rather interesting to explain why they were up there in the first place, as it wasn't like they could just claim they got lost.

But their eyes weren't met with any developers or workers at KCON period. It wasn't an empty room either, which would have been disappointing, but definitely less nerve-wracking.

"Hey, stop!" Jinhwan yells, and the conversation that had been going on between the two was left behind in any instant. 

Both of them run into the room, making a bolt at the figure. There was a black cap over their face, preventing anything but their eyes and mouth from behind seen. From their body shape, however, despite their baggy clothing, it was clear it was a woman like they all assumed.

"Who the fuck are you?!" Jungkook is demanding as the two of them corner off the lady. She has a duffel bag over her shoulder, and they had a good feeling of what it contained. 

Hearts beating out of their chests, they try to figure out a way to approach her. If she got away, that was it. This was their only chance to end this once and for all.

Not a word leaves the woman's mouth, she only peers at them with narrowed eyes. If she wanted to say something, she would've, right? Why was she silent?

"Give us the bag," Jinhwan demands as he steps forward, holding out his hand and waiting for his request to be fulfilled.

"And I'd remove the cap if I were you," Jungkook hums from just behind him, cracking one of his knuckles, "I want you to see me clearly when I break every fucking limb in your fat fucking bo-"

"HEY!" Jinhwan yells, leaping forward as he tries to grab her. The two of them hadn't noticed the fire exit escape she'd been trying to itch towards, and had jumped at. 

Realizing what was happening, that she was getting away, Jungkook feels a lump get caught in his throat. Not knowing what to do, he fiddles for his phone as the lady had slammed the door back, and a click sounds from outside, indicating she locked it. So that was how she got in here in the first place.

Dialing the first number he sees, he holds it to his ear, hoping it was answered before it was too late. Jinhwan was messing with the door, slamming his shoulder against it as he curses, "why the fuck is it not opening? She jammed something in the lock from the outside," he realizes a second later when it didn't budge. 

Completely fed up with the fact they'd been so close, he kicks the concrete door out of anger, as if it would make any difference, "god fucking dammit!"

"H-Hello?" Jungkook nearly drops his phone from the small voice, he hadn't noticed he called her out of all people.

Either way, there was no time for him to worry about it.

"Mi, I need you to listen carefully," he didn't bother with a greeting, speaking as fast as he could form thoughts in his head.

But the girl is a mess of confusion, "huh? Jungkook, what are you talking about, is there something wro-"

"- Go outside, whoever is after you is bolting through the parking lot right now. You have to catch them, Mi, they have baggy clothes on and they're trying to leave," he cuts her off, blurting out everything before she could even have time to process what he was saying, "you have to go now, it's your only chance."

His urges sent her into a state of shock. Was he serious?

But after a second, when he only continues his calls to her, telling her she had to move if she wanted to end it, she knew it wasn't any sort of sick joke. That was what he was planning.

"I'm going," she tells him harshly before ending the call, shoving her phone in her pocket. 

The New York sun beams down on Soomi as she pushes out the metal exit doors. It didn't matter if anyone saw her leave, she didn't care. This was life or death to her even if that was overdramatic, she wasn't letting them get away.

Heading out into the private parking, located at the back of the arena where fans weren't allowed, her head whips every which way. "Where are you?" she whispers out, as if it would help her spot them any easier. Her heart is beating out of her chest, dragging along with her as she runs through the parking lot, raking her eyes across every inch of it as she tries to spot the monster that was making her life a living hell.

Now or never, her mind kept yelling at her, you can't let them get away.

Jungkook had done what he could, now it was her turn to fight her own battle. And ending it is exactly what she was going to do.

"Hey!" she screams at the sight of a figure. Using what she knew of them, she takes in everything. 

Baggy clothes, female, carrying a massive bag.

Bingo.

"Hey!" she yells louder, her fists balling at her side as she breaks into a run. Realizing she was wearing heels because she'd been dressed for the show, she rips them off her feet so she could run faster across the concrete. It burned the soles of her feet from the flaming sun, and the pieces of dirt and rock cut her feet as she goes, but it only makes her force herself to run faster, "STOP!"

Only noticing her now, the figure had turned around to peer at her. But she wasn't wearing a cap to cover her face like she had been when she was caught by Jungkook and Jinhwan.

And Soomi knew exactly who she was.

"HEY," she screams, trying to hide the astonishment on her face as she runs. The psycho seemed to realize the fact she was caught because Soomi had no doubt seen her face. A look of defeat had taken over it, before she spins on her heel and makes a bolt for her vehicle, probably thinking that she could still blackmail her anyway.

But Soomi was too determined, she was too outrageously angered. Nothing could compare to the boiling of seething infuriation in her veins. It was an emotion she'd never felt in her life, and she reaches her arm back, throwing the heel in her hand straight at the woman's head.

It hits with a clap before falling to the ground behind her. A screech leaves the lady's lips, and the split moment of shock that had taken over her from being hit Soomi used to her advantage.

"You fucking bitch!" the familiar voice cries as she's tackled to the ground.

If anyone ever thought Soomi was weak, they should see her now. It was no joke the woman was stronger than her, but with the immense furious feeling that was inside of her, she could probably beat up Jungkook if she wanted to.

Grabbing both of her wrists with her hands, she holds them over her head as she keeps her body on the ground with her own. Meeting the eyes of the woman, she could only gawk in disbelief, "y-you're iKON's manager, what the fuck is wrong with you?!" she yells in astonishment, the anger making her eyes nearly bloodshot, "you've put me through so much shit and for what, you fucking psycho?!"

Not saying anything, her breath is heavy as she tries to fight off the girl's anger. But Soomi picks up one of her heels, slamming the sharp heel into her arm. A scream echoes through the air, and the girl hisses again, "don't try to get away bitch, you're going straight to jail for what you've caused," she snaps, "hurting your own artist, how could you do that, you sick fuck?!"

Trying to catch her breath as she was in pain from the attack on her arm, she finally spoke.

"I did it because I had to, so maybe you would stop putting his career in jeopardy you selfish whore-" Soomi slams the heel into her arm again, and this time it cut skin, but it only cut her off for a second. "These poor boys fall at your feet, just for you to use them like pieces of dirt, but yet YG sees you as this angel, it makes me fucking sick!"

"You don't deserve any of this, I know what you've done, you fucking drug-addict," she screams as if someone would hear her in the middle of the parking lot, "I know what kind of person you really are, we don't want you in Korea just like your own parents didn't!"

When the woman looks to her again, her eyes are red. You could barely even see that bright green in her irises, almost like something supernatural was taking over her.

Just like your own parents didn't.

"You bitch, you're going to feel real pain you fucking-" Soomi had raised the heel of her shoe, again meaning she removed one hand from the woman's wrist. It was about to head straight into one of her eyes, where she would then go for the other. She wanted this woman to hurt, she wanted her to bleed, to be left a mess of agony on the ground. 

Just as the shoe is heading straight for her eye, the woman grabs Soomi's wrist with her free hand, stopping her. Having been saving her strength, the petite girl screeches when she flips her over, her back hitting the concrete with a hard thump.

An ache shoots up her spine from the impact, and she struggles to rip the woman's hand off of her. "What was that now?" she mocks with a devious laugh as she towers over her, "you seemed to forget you're nothing but a child, sweet Soomi."

Eyes flaming, she tries again to rip her wrists out of her hand, "fuck you, I'm going to fucking-"

"- Aw, you're going to what now?" the girl's eyes bulge at the sound of something cocking, and she gasps at the sight of just that - a gun.

At the welling fear that takes over her expression despite how she tries to hide it, the woman bursts into fits of booming laughter. She laughed like she never had before, like this was the best moment of her entire life. Really, it was, she'd been waiting for such a great time for as long as she could remember.

All her years of following the girl, they all added up to now.

Taking out the world's trash, one at a time. And it all started with Kim Soomi.

Or should she say Solar Kim?

"Not so brave now, are we?" she taunts, unable to hold in her laughter. The barrel of the gun is cold against Soomi's head, and she winces from the feeling. Trying one last time to get out of her grip, her strength was just too much compared to her, she'd been tricked, and she had to face it.

"Let this be a valuable lesson for you, you should go over it daily wherever you end up rotting," her finger is just hovering over the trigger, and not knowing what else she could do, Soomi squeezes her eyes shut.

She waits, she waits for the inevitable, she waits for everything she had built to crumble before her. Not because she would get exposed, or everyone would know how she really was back then, but because the legacy of Kim Soomi, Korea's number one solo artist, the idol that had taken the industry over night, and the girl who loved more than she could manage, would be gone.

Soomi knew it was it for her.

Until nothing happened.
